Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
9
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

6   Preface

1)
Words Given During the Distribution of the Stone of Blessing
<Summary of Words> The motto of the Teacher’s life was to be God’s spokesperson. From today, I ask that you become heavenly spokespersons. And be God’s representatives. Furthermore, I hope you will become God’s ambassadors. 
This stone is a condition of the three realms, given by the Teacher and received by you, so deeply commemorate and cherish it in your hearts.
The name of this stone is the Stone of Blessing. 
From now on, do not criticize or complain about the Teacher’s work (the members promised this with cheers). Those close to the Teacher cannot let go of their hearts until they die. Forget everything you have done until now. And from now on, be careful. 
Regarding the Father’s heart, you must become the weakest of the weak. 
Looking back, most of heaven’s work has been a journey of tears. * 
March 13, 1960 (Sun), after the Sunday service at the former headquarters church. 
* This summary of words is taken from the unnumbered words published in <Seonghwa> No. 25.

2)
Life Centered on the Three Great Kingships
<Summary of Words> Our immediate goal is principled preparation, character training, and heart training. From now on, our life and activities must be centered on the three great kingships of the region. The three great kingships of the region are the center, and all other organizations are auxiliary to this. 
In judgment, there are three types: word judgment, character judgment, and heart judgment. We are now entering the stage of character training, having passed the stage of principled preparation through the word. 
To become a person of character, organized training is necessary. One must go through collective family life (like in apartments). The question is whether one can pass through the overall ideology or system. One must pass through such gateways. 
It is good for the small group meetings of the three great kingship unit to rotate among each member's home. Strengthen horizontal relationships through these meetings. New members should be guided by the group leaders to be placed and integrated into each region. 
Soon, we will create a prayer for the church’s victory. What pleases heaven is to fight on the front lines and achieve results. In the future, small group meetings should be held at the class level. As we develop further, we will center on the three great kingships, and when this expands to 12 people, we must split again. Communication should take the form of 3 levels above and 3 levels below, in a 7-unit structure. 
In the future, any judgment regarding events must be resolved within the environmental limits. For example, if it is a matter of the three great kingships, it must be resolved within the class, group, and region. The headquarters will also have jurisdiction down to the region, group, and class. 
As much as possible, the three great kingships should live and die together so as not to depend on the upper levels. Hurting the upper levels brings heaven’s sorrow, while hurting Satan brings heaven’s glory. 
The people at the headquarters must be emotionally united with the front-line members. In the future, just as you listen to the Teacher’s words, you must absolutely listen to the words of the regional leaders or group leaders. 
In the future, the headquarters will send out traveling evangelists to provide care. 
In every nation or ethnic group, if the front-line soldiers and the citizens in the rear unite their hearts and exert effort, they will surely prosper. There must be a watchman at the group level who can await orders. Abandon the idea of trying to look good to someone. Whether it works or not, be loyal according to your own abilities. Even if you gather within the three great kingships, three people should not gather alone. We must ensure that 12 people gather as soon as possible. * 
3)
Words Given on the First Parents’ Day
<Summary of Words> The issues of life and the path to eternal life are principled and very complex. Even retrieving money deposited in a bank involves procedures and complicated steps; how much more complex is the path to eternal life, which involves retrieving a life that has already died? 
You do not know all the procedures, and it is difficult, so the most precious and wise way is to fulfill the way of obedience. 
In nature, we see that in spring, new leaves sprout abundantly. However, what is necessary and important there is not the leaves but the stem that produces those leaves. Similarly, in Christianity, cutting off the stem of life leads to ruin. 
God’s restoration history can also be seen as a history to establish true parents. Therefore, from Cain and Abel to today, heaven has been providentially working internally to restore true parents. Anyone who opposes or hinders this fundamental providence (the central stem) to achieve this purpose will be forsaken before the heavenly way and will ultimately perish. 
Even if one pushes forward with their work in an environment where all conditions are established, it often leads to failure; how can one be confident in doing heavenly work? Faith that merely vaguely believes it will go to heaven, faith that unconditionally believes it has been saved, and shallow faith are wrong. Therefore, one must not relax for even a minute or a second and must walk the difficult and narrow path of life while connecting with the Father. 
Just as a person has a heart door, there is also a door that connects to the heavenly castle. Therefore, in doing heavenly work, one must not miss the timing and must pass through that door. At this time, it is essential to study and pray about where to call the Father from, what heart to have when seeking the Father, and which of the Father’s hearts to inherit first. 
God is the essence of love and is just. No matter how wicked a person may be, they will be guided along the path at least three times through that heart. Since human nature is oriented toward heaven, even the most wicked person is given the opportunity to find the path of life through God’s influence. Throughout one’s life, heaven will come at least three times; if one misses this opportunity, the way to connect with heaven will be severed. 
We must realize that our mission differs when we are infants, when we grow, and after we have grown to inherit God’s great legacy. The Father cannot raise us forever. We must realize and grow to share in the Father’s work. Should we not grow quickly to do the Father’s work? 
Loyalty and filial piety are not taught to be performed; they must arise from the heart and be done automatically. Moreover, one must not offer sincerity before heaven by hearing or learning from others; it must come from one’s own heart. * 
4)
Whose Sons and Daughters Are You?
Romans 8:12-21
<Prayer> At this time, please allow us to harmonize with the original heart of the Father as it is felt in our hearts. 
Father, please help us to know what position we are in and to realize where we, who want to boast and show off, stand. In the historical path that goes through the past and present toward the future, and within the laws of heaven and earth, what position have we taken, what have we become that we want to show off, and how have we asserted our own value? Please help us to examine ourselves at this time. 
We have felt deeply that the path we have walked in life is one without a place to settle. We cannot deny that we are wandering without knowing where to rest our hearts during this one hour. We have already felt that those who dream of a day of rest while holding onto such a self will inevitably become losers in the journey of life. The sorrowful me longs for life, and the grieving me is distressed because I do not know the path, and the wandering me is wandering to reach a single destination. 
Our hands have not grasped anything that can break and overcome the power of death, and our hearts have not established a center that can be directly connected to the heavenly world. 
All beings in heaven and earth cannot exist outside the laws of heaven, and we are pitiful beings who are not affiliated with heaven. Please allow us to know how to lament over such a self. The self that wants to boast is an empty existence, and the self that judges by comparison is close to being judged when viewed from a heavenly position. I earnestly hope and desire this. 
The Father has the responsibility to resolve the sorrow of those who are lost in life, not knowing their position, value, or direction. The garden of rest where all people should dwell, a place of value that can be boasted of before all creation, is the place I have been searching for, the place of eternal life, and I know that the Father is working hard today to find that place where all humanity can joyfully run with both hands raised. 
We know that the Father has worked hard to accomplish this until now, will work hard in this age, and will worry about the future. 
Now, with what face shall we meet the Father? How shall we serve the Father? How shall we long for the Father? How shall we wish to hear the Father’s words? We do not know that. 
We have become a lowly appearance, worse than a lump of clay, due to the fall. Please lead us to a time when we do not consider our own existence or allow any of our own subjectivity or consciousness. 
Let us transcend our own concepts and consciousness and become like the clay held in Your hands, able to be molded as You wish and respond according to Your will. I earnestly hope and desire that You may grant us the touch of re-creation so that we can belong again to the Father’s dominion and have the pulse of life beat within us. 
The Father said He created all things in heaven and earth through His words, so please allow the bodies that were dead to be resurrected through the Father’s words, so that we may sing of their value in joy before all creation. And may the joy and glory of the Father explode deep within our hearts, allowing us to experience the appearance of freedom filled with joy at this time. We ask for nothing more than this one purpose, this one heart, this one work to be deeply rooted in our hearts. 
Now, Father, You have appeared to speak; what shall I say? In the past, I have spoken many words. You know that there have been many times when I had to speak even in environments where I could not speak, so may this time not be such a time. May we admire with our hearts, rejoice with our hearts, and may Your sorrow become our sorrow, Your situation become our situation, and Your sadness become our sadness. Please allow this time to be one where we can leap into the place of the Father’s glory with all our heart and sincerity. 
Now, may all that I wish to convey be entrusted to You, Father. 
May the hearts of the giver and the receiver become one, transcending all consciousness and temporal concepts, and may this time be one where we can feel the movement of the Father who moves personally. May this hour be one where we can unknowingly dwell in the shadow of the deep heart of the Father, and I earnestly request that You allow us to have such an experience. 
Please bless all of humanity who desire the grace of blessing on this day, and bless the many altars. Especially bless those hidden sons and daughters of Yours who are exhausted from fighting in lonely battle, kneeling before the Father’s presence, longing for the time and season. 
Since You are the Father who seeks to establish the same grace, I earnestly request that You bless us to be able to face the grace of glory in the same victorious form at this time. I pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. 
16   Whose Sons and Daughters Are You?
<Words> The title of the words I wish to present to you at this time is "Whose Sons and Daughters Are You?" I will speak on the topic of whose children you are. 
The Root of Good and Evil
We know that due to the connection of the fall, humanity is under the shadow of death.
individuals have not yet appeared. 

We must leave this state. We must organize the environment we find ourselves in. How? If the body resists, we must strike through it. If the heart resists, we must push through it. If our feelings obstruct the path, we must break through those feelings. This path of pioneering is the path of virtue. The path of virtue is the way of letting go, the way of breaking through, the way of forgetting everything and moving forward.

For thousands of years, we have been told to seek, yet no one has gone, and no one has claimed victory. Throughout history, countless people have tried to break free from the lineage of lamentation, to discard the name of sinful children and take on the name of good children, but still, there is no evidence of victory. The problem lies here.

If there is a heaven and a hell, then heaven and hell exist within our hearts. We stand at the crossroads of death and rebirth, where good and evil are in conflict. While you tremble at the global fears of the end times, if you are someone who longs for true life and seeks the true homeland, you must recognize that the external fears are not the real issue; it is the struggle between good and evil within your own heart that is far more terrifying.

If you become a loser here, you will never escape the bloodline of evil parents, becoming a child of the world of death. But if you win, you will stand as a child of heavenly parents, recognized by heaven, becoming a child who remains in the world of divine value that transcends earthly history. Therefore, we must hold onto our hearts and fight. This struggle cannot be resolved by any external entity; it must be resolved from within our own hearts. That is why when Jesus was asked where heaven is, he replied, "Heaven is within your heart." 

No matter how conscientious or good a person may be, if their heart does not continue to live in harmony with the universe and sing praises to that parent throughout their life, they will be cut off and blocked. 

We are the ones who must go. Even if we dislike it, history is moving toward that destination, and even if we do not wish to go, this world is moving toward that destination. If any nation betrays the fate of the world, heaven will drive that nation out. If any individual stands against the direction of fate and refuses to go, heaven will push them aside and continue moving toward the purpose of the great universe. We must go toward that destination.

We often say that when someone represents our country in an international competition, they are referred to as the children of Korea. Furthermore, when someone represents a group or a tribe within the nation, they are called the children of that group or tribe. Additionally, when entering a family, they are referred to as the children of their parents. Thus, the term "children" is used broadly. 

Then, what should be the path of true children? We have not become children recognized by heaven. The standard for such children does not exist on this earth. It is not present. This can be affirmed. There is no standard that can be called children of a nation recognized by heaven. Is there such a standard? No, there is not. Since the creation of heaven and earth, there has been no law or guideline that can be called children of a family, tribe, or nation recognized by heaven.

Has the nation of Israel become children of heaven? No, it has not. They often betrayed heaven and consistently walked the path of rebellion against heaven throughout the ages, even killing the Messiah who was sent. They could not stand in a position where God could say, "You are my children who represent the world." They could not stand in a position as children of heaven who established a nation on behalf of heaven, nor could they stand as children of heaven representing a tribe. Furthermore, they could not even claim to be children of heaven centered around a family. 

If anyone believes they have achieved this, please raise your hand. This is the problem. When we think about this, heaven appears to be pitiful. What has heaven longed for with heartfelt desire? It must have been to establish unfallen humans, our unfallen ancestors, as global children. Surely, heaven dreamed of establishing children who could govern the world and represent the sovereignty of nations, as well as children of tribes or families.

However, because all the standards heaven sought to establish have been severed, human life has become a struggle and a source of suffering. Therefore, we must kick away the iron bars of the devil and greet the day of liberation by seeking the parents whom heaven can recognize. When we think of this, it is truly astonishing; there is nothing more astonishing than this. Heaven has labored for 6,000 years and woven an altar of unspeakable sacrifice, yet individuals who can hold such a standard have not yet appeared.
What do you mean by not being in your position? We must realize that we should lament.  
The will of God is carried out by those who are oppressed.  
We have gathered. We came together without caring about the path of persecution. We have come. We came without caring about the valley of sorrow. Why? We came to escape from the children of this evil world and to become true children of goodness.  
Our ancestors, who have come and gone throughout history, organized their environment and set out towards their destination, which was an action and practice in accordance with God's command.  
Look. What about Grandpa Noah? He was pressed by his environment. However, he built the ark for 120 years, pouring all his passion and wealth into it. He worked with all his heart and, whenever he had time, he shouted that in 120 years, the world would be judged by water. For 120 years he cried out, but he could not find a single follower. Countless crowds mocked him. They laughed at him looking up at the clear sky and sighed at him on the street. Noah was mocked and oppressed like that. He wanted to be part of the new family of the new nation, the new parents, and the new kin, cutting off all ties with the world. This is the standard of loyalty that God desires. But do you think you can just believe and go to heaven? That won't do.  
What about Abraham? He left Ur of the Chaldeans and, without hesitation, happily abandoned his beloved hometown and all his possessions to go into the wilderness. This is the kind of step our ancestor of faith, Abraham, took. Look at Moses as well. He abandoned everything and led 600,000 people into the wilderness. There, he too was oppressed. Throughout history, the saints and sages who have advocated goodness have been driven out of the world. Only after being driven out can one fulfill their purpose. Therefore, we must be driven and driven. We must reach the destination we need to go to, which is the position of parents centered on God.  
Among the words we read today, there is the phrase that we are God's adopted children. There are those who comfort themselves by saying, "I believe in Jesus, so I will go to heaven, and I attend church, so I am a child of God," but the children of God I know are not such people. If God's heart from before creation to the end of time is deeply ingrained in my bones, and if there is sorrow in God, I should be able to feel that sorrow with life, and if there is joy, I should be able to feel that joy with life. In other words, I must be able to communicate with all of God's emotions to be determined as a child of God; it cannot happen before that. Can you become an adopted child in this world just by calling someone "Father"? No, that is not the case. To become a child of heaven, you must enter a position where you can emotionally call God "Father" by receiving the heavenly lineage. Before that, you are like a servant. You have no relationship with the True Parents. You are an adopted child because the lineage is different.  
The realization that we thought these were our parents, but they are our enemies! This realization is the providence of salvation that allows us to cut off ties with this enemy of a different lineage.  
History has been made by those who are oppressed. We must understand that all those who have led the world and advocated ideas or thoughts have been oppressed. Individuals are oppressed by their tribes, feeling something new and struggling to follow the heart of the great ancestors of heaven and earth; this is the course of history. If there are historians who observe history, they must observe it from that perspective. If they do not know that history flows based on the invisible heart of heaven's providence, they are not true historians. History flows under the emotional ideology that created the great Creator. It cannot be denied that it moves under a clear purpose.  
It has formed from clans to tribes, through nations, and further through allied nations to form a union. Now the time is near. The time to open the doors of the world is gradually approaching us.  
Then, what kind of standard should emerge in the future? Since God, who created the universe, is our Father, a prince must rise who can confidently say that this world is mine, standing in the position of His son or daughter. This is what heaven and earth desire.  
The Way of the Tao  
What did humanity lose with the fall? They lost the land. Humanity has become one that has lost the land. This land has become a land without a master, trampled here and there by the ideologies and movements of this nation and that nation. Thus, humanity has also become a masterless humanity. At times, this ideology sweeps through, and at other times, that ideology sweeps through, resulting in masterless humanity, and furthermore, the heavens have also become a masterless heaven.  
Therefore, we are seeking the master. We are seeking the parents.  
O land, stained with blood for 6,000 years, O humanity that has been trampled, O heaven that has sighed because of this land and humanity, we must create a world where heaven can cry, humanity can cry, and the land can cry. If there is a Creator, it must surely be so. If it does not happen, then God does not exist.  
Since we are taking steps to find our parents, we cannot remain still until we meet those parents.  
History passes. For several centuries, it has chosen and embraced certain nations, only to let them go. Now, globally, democracy and communism are in confrontation. This may seem like the role of the ultimate parents, but it is not. Those who are fighting cannot be true parents. They are false. There cannot be two masters centered on emotions. When it comes to singing centered on emotions, there is only one. Where is the brave one who can conquer the heart of the parents on this earth? Even if there is a great king or a powerful ruler, they cannot invade that.  
God can say to you, "You are my sons and daughters," and you can say to Him, "You are my Father." This emotional world must be established in the end times. If there are people who live according to such standards emotionally and practically, they will be victorious. There will be no one who can conquer them.  
That is why we must go today as well. Isn't that right, everyone? Humans have fallen parents but do not have unfallen parents. No matter how proud they are, no matter how good they think they are, they are descendants of fallen ancestors. They are a race of fall. The elements of evil are deeply rooted and have flowed from ancestors to permeate your very being. Do you think that such a body, doing whatever it wants, will bring joy to heaven? No. It must be denied. You must deny what you see, what you hear, what you eat, and even what you sleep. The way of the Tao is such a path. It does not acknowledge. It does not tolerate any concept of ownership. You must cut off even the notion of whose son or daughter you are. Where is such a law? Even the parents who gave birth to me cannot be recognized as true parents by heaven, so they must be cut off. The same goes for spouses and children.  
That is why Jesus said, "Anyone who does not love me more than anyone else cannot be my disciple." The Tao begins from here. The true Tao denies even the concept of emotional ownership. A high religion centered on emotions lives like one in prison. It denies even the emotional ownership of humans. Therefore, anything else is not a problem.  
We must deny everything. We must deny it a thousand times, ten thousand times. We must completely deny these eyes, these ears, this stomach, and these emotions. O God! If you are alive, strike me so that I may completely deny myself. This is the life of a Taoist. The purpose of judgment is to raise and move things when there is nothing left to strike.  
Then, how will we settle the emotional ties that are blood-related? This is likely the greatest hardship of heaven. Situations can be resolved easily, but emotions can only be resolved by risking life and death. Situations can be resolved by establishing conditions of relative value, but emotional issues can only be resolved by risking my absolute life. That is why the way of the Tao must be walked with death at stake.  
Parents We Must Find  
We are in a destiny that must start. Before God, who has worked for 6,000 years, we must say with a heart full of sorrow, "Father, who has come to find humanity."  
We must be able to do so. God, who has struggled for a long 6,000 years, seeking children, has followed humanity with a sorrowful heart, crying out. We must understand that only by becoming such a person can we enter the kingdom of God.  
Look. God has worked for 6,000 years, yet there are still no sons and daughters whom He can embrace and love forever. How can we not lament this? Everyone, do you feel this in your heart? Can God come into your home and say, "Come, serve me. Come, I will sleep in your house"? It cannot be. God has not had a person to dwell in, nor has He had a home. Isn’t it written in 1 Corinthians 3:16? "Do you not know that you are the temple of God?" The temple refers to a house. God is seeking a house. The denomination is for the purpose of building a house. What is the purpose of the house? It is to find sons and daughters. We seek to enter the house so that we can find sons and daughters. Ultimately, it is about finding sons and daughters.  
At one time, I prayed like this:  
"Father! If the fate of the great universe is alive, I can understand your deep parental heart, so please make me a son or daughter who can enjoy with you in one family, as you wish."  
Have you ever prayed like this? The Father, who has longed for sons and daughters for 6,000 years, must be saying, "O my son and daughter," and in that moment, He must be struggling, not knowing whether to rejoice or cry, embracing and enjoying that moment. Have you ever welcomed such a Father? You have not, have you?  
We still have a path to walk. We have the mission to find the parents of our family, and at the same time, we have the mission to find the parents of our tribe. We also have the mission to find the parents of our nation. We have the mission to find the parents of our country. Furthermore, we have the mission to find the parents of the world and the parents of heaven and earth.  
A loyal person who is prepared to give their life for their nation does not hesitate to deny their own parents and their own spouse. The current time is passing through the era of nationalism. Now, we must go beyond the era of nationalism centered on tribes and embrace new parents centered on the world. The time is approaching when we must welcome global parents beyond national parents. We must become loyal subjects. We must become filial sons and daughters. We must become virtuous women. Ultimately, what kind of parents must we welcome? We must welcome the Creator who created heaven and earth, surpassing the parents of the world. We humans must go to the position where we can welcome such parents. That path is the path of sorrow. We must understand that it is a sorrowful hill that we must struggle to overcome.  
In carrying out the providence of salvation, God did not first send the parents of the world. He did not send the parents of the nation. He did not send the parents of the tribe. He did not send the parents of any religion. He started from the position of an individual parent. He began with one household. He sought a resting place for His presence, starting from one household.  
The Savior who comes as the global parent  
The Abel's altar and Noah's family were what came out of that search, but because it was broken, the traces of 1,600 years of labor vanished without a trace. After 400 years of labor, He tried to find it again centered on Abraham's family, but because Abraham made a mistake with the offering, it was broken again. It was only when it reached Jacob, the third generation through Isaac, that God could establish the goal of family and carry out His providence. Look closely at the Bible. God wanted to bless the nation He chose on this earth, but He could not do so and instead blessed Jacob's household. He only sought one household of Jacob that could lead. It was a sorrowful history. What is the ancestor of faith? It is the new root of faith. He wanted to multiply and establish a nation centered on Jacob's household, but in the end, He could not fulfill that purpose either.  
What happened to the descendants of Jacob, who received the blessing of the family? They fell in the wilderness. How could Moses have known that they would fall in the wilderness when he led the oppressed people out of Egypt? Moses was placed in the position of the parents of the nation. If the Israelite people had acted with the heart of "I will die with you, I will live with you, where my father goes, how can I not go?" they would not have perished. However, the foundation on which Moses was established as the parent of the nation was broken without a trace.  
Thus, those who were established by inheriting the lineage of tribal parents became numerous prophets. What kind of parents came on that foundation? They come as the parents of the world, surpassing the parents of the nation and further becoming the parents of heaven and earth. This is the thought of the Savior, the thought of the Messiah. You must understand this clearly. Then, what is the purpose of the Messiah's coming? It is to break the evil nation and its sovereignty and to establish the sovereignty of goodness so that God can govern the world.  
Jesus came before all humanity. How? He established Jacob as a family parent type, Moses as a national parent type, and then sent Jesus as a global parent type before the Israelite people. To be a parent, one must enter the world of enemies, fight, and win. That is why Jacob went to Laban's household in Haran and fought. Moses also entered the palace of Pharaoh, the world of enemies, and fought. It is only by fighting and winning that one can determine their position as a parent. Jesus also had to come to this world, like the land of Egypt in Moses' time, and fight to find the standard of a global parent. But he died. He left in failure. Because he failed, he must come again.  
What was intended to establish global parents has failed, so the familial parents and national parents have all been broken as well.  
Because the standard of parents, which had been sought through 4,000 years of work and the laws of heaven and earth, has been lost, we must spiritually connect with those parents. That is why Jesus spoke of the bride and bridegroom. Do you know what the Holy Spirit is? It is the Mother. Today, in Christianity, people do not even know what the Holy Spirit is, yet they keep saying Holy Spirit, Holy Spirit, but the Holy Spirit is the Mother. Jesus is the Son God, and God is the Father God. Because the sons and daughters cannot be true parents before the Father and have fallen, Jesus came as the True Parent to give birth to you again.  
What is rebirth? It is to be born again. To be born again means that one has died, right? One must come out again from the womb of the Mother, the Holy Spirit.
purpose is to establish the true parents. Once you have a blood relationship with that parent, you cannot deny God. You will not be able to deny the existence of God’s world even in your dreams. The Father resides within me, and I enter into the realm where the Father is present in my life. We must understand that Heaven calls us to meet the parents who will transfer us into that emotional world.

No matter what path or providence it may be, the ultimate purpose is to serve the parents. If there is love, where can there be a greater love than that? Ultimately, God becomes the parent. Look at the Bible. It speaks of humans who have lost their parents, of humans like orphans and widows. That is why we are moving toward a world where we can serve God as our parent. That place is the ultimate destination of life.

The sins of our ancestors, Adam and Eve
Therefore, the title I wish to speak to you about today is the providence of restoration aimed at completing the resolution of the heart. I will speak under the title of the providence of restoration aimed at completing the resolution of the heart. 

Among you, there may be some who have worshiped heaven for 10 or 20 years, or even spent a lifetime seeking the path of virtue. What is the reason you are walking this difficult path? It is not because you have done wrong. More than your own mistakes, there is a mistake with our ancestors, and if we trace back to those ancestors, there is a fundamental wrongdoer, which is Adam and Eve, the ancestors of fallen humanity. 

Our ancestors, Adam and Eve, grew up in the embrace of God’s love and were nurtured under the heart of God’s most sacred and great love. However, no matter how cute their growing appearance was and how free their living environment was, there was something they did not possess. What was that? It was not that there were no granted possessions, nor that there were no servants. It was that Adam and Eve could not establish a heart connection to become the sons and daughters of God. That is their grievance.

If you want to know more specific and detailed things, come here and listen to the words. This is not a lie. Since you have lost your body (substance) on earth, you must find that body on earth. Therefore, it is only natural that the True Parents, that is, the Lord, must come in the flesh. Those who oppose this are stones. They are people with hardened heads. This is a natural statement. No ancestor who has come and gone on this earth for 6,000 years knew this.

Who are our ancestors? They are fallen beings. From the perspective of the fallen world, ancestors are ancestors, but from a heavenly perspective, those who come later are the ancestors. The later ones are the ancestors. You must understand this. It is when a global parent emerges, a global family emerges, and a global sovereignty emerges. This world must be overcome. But does that mean it must perish? I am also one of those who pray for that.

Now you know where your hearts are running. Where does the heart run? If there is someone who has established a heartistic standard and can pass through the heart of their parents, then even though they are on earth, they have the authority to command the spirit world. Is that so or not? The spirit world is the first Israel. It is equivalent to the world of angels before the fall. Because Jesus restored spiritually in the form of the angelic world just before the fall, the spirits who remain within the realm of paradise are equivalent to angels. Because I know this principle, the person speaking here has also fought many battles with the spirit world. When you establish the standard of victory from those battles, you will be given the authority to command many spirits in the spirit world from the earth. You will be able to govern the angels in heaven. Only then will Satan flee. Satan will flee.

You put everything into your womb and stuff everything into your head.
Oh! Call upon the name of the Lord and shout as much as you can. Will it work? It won't. It cannot happen until the standard of heart is established. Do you think that if you create a document on your own and go before God saying, "I am your son" or "I am your daughter," it will be effective? Absolutely not. From what I know and believe, calling upon the Father is not that simple. When you have the authority to command and move everything in the spiritual world based on the standard of heart, Satan will flee. You must become such a person. To do that, you need to have the initiative of heart. That is the principle.

A world governed by a group centered on heart
When such sons and daughters are born on this earth, the entire Christian world on earth, that is, the Second Israel, will be governed. Only then will the history of unification unfold. It means being governed. No matter how much you struggle and act out, in the end, you will be defeated. Isn't that satisfying? That is the true God. If God is the one who decides victory and defeat by power, what use is such a God? If that were the case, it wouldn't take 6,000 years for the restoration providence.

When God moves, He moves; when He decides, He decides; when God is sad, His sons and daughters must be able to feel that sadness, and when God cries, they must be able to cry endlessly. When God is joyful, they must be able to dance without thinking of their own dignity. Earlier, when Elder Song laughed during prayer, those who saw it for the first time might have thought it was funny. However, the one who laughed is the one who is truly funny.

The restoration history to complete the resolution of heart begins with you. The restoration of heart does not start from heaven, nor from the world, but from your own heart. How incredible is that? It is not the heavenly world. It is not this world. It is your heart. The place where the resolution of heart is completed is where the individual longs for the value of the whole, and the whole sings the value of the individual. Did Jesus not say, "I am in the Father, and you are in me, and I am in you"?

Centered on the standard of heart, even if the value is small, it can transcend the limitations of time, space, and distance and stand boldly in comparison to the value of the whole. One strand of hair from a loved one is more precious than a million diamonds. Isn't that so? One who has such a standard belongs to heaven. In front of such a person, no matter how much you tell them not to, Satan cannot help but flee. This is because of the laws of heaven.

When such sons and daughters of heart appear, the families formed by those sons and daughters, the nations formed by those sons and daughters, and the world formed by those sons and daughters must become a place where our Father becomes the King of Kings and reigns forever. You must become His sons and daughters. You must be the sons and daughters of heart, the historical sons and daughters. The heart is the same whether it is a thousand years ago or a thousand years later.

For 6,000 years, God has struggled, disregarding the mountains and rugged valleys. The grief of that God must be resolved in our generation. To resolve that, we must first understand the historical heart and be able to hold onto the heart of the True Parents, True Couples, and True Siblings. The joy of that is not the joy of heaven but the joy that my body can sing, the joy that is tangible. When my individual value becomes a universal value and if I say, "Follow me," you must be able to say, "Yes, I will follow you. Yes, I will praise you."

Only when sons and daughters who can stand on such a standard arise will God's desire, who created all things and blessed them, be fulfilled. Only then will God's sorrowful heart, which seeks to find fallen humanity again, be resolved, and finally, a garden of freedom where He can embrace and love His beloved sons and daughters will be opened.

The first gateway is the True Parents.
Awake, sleeping humanity! The time has come to shout. The True Parents, who were lost 6,000 years ago, are coming back to this earth. Heaven has worked so hard to send that Parent, to send the beloved Son as a gift. To send that Parent, God has pierced through Satan's nets, broken through the depths of hell, shed blood, endured beatings, and has come out in anguish and weeping. We must clearly understand that God is the Lord of the universe and the King who has struggled until now.

We must comfort that God. That God has longed to judge all worldly matters at once, but because He has a purpose, a desire, and a hope on this earth, He has been looking at it and enduring, enduring, and enduring. You must call that God your Father. You must call the God of heart, not just in name, your Father. Thus, our non-blood relatives, non-parents, and non-siblings must be mobilized globally to establish the heavenly principles and connect with the heart of heaven, transcending time and space, nations and states, and a new Lord centered on the heart of heaven must emerge on this earth. If that does not happen, the world will break apart.

The person shouting here today knows that fact, which is why they are doing this. If you do not know this, you will all perish. If even one person among the 30 million people or the 2.7 billion people in the world knows and acts on this, the world will be conquered by that person. The world will become that person's world, that person's nation. It can be concluded with certainty that the world will become a world that such a group can govern.

<Prayer> No matter how many sorrows there are in the situation of coming and going, I know that history cannot be resolved by holding onto that and crying. Even if one does not know how to cry, if there is someone who steps forward for the Father with a heart, that person will inherit the Father's will and be established before the Father. May these people, through the words they have heard today, deeply taste new joy in their hearts and have an amazing experience of heart, realizing, "This is the value of humanity, this is the meaning of the Bible, this is how the connections of the world have come to be, this is the content of the heart of heaven." 

If this is the center of the words, the purpose of humanity, the purpose of the world, and the purpose of God, then if you have this standard, God will meet you, humanity will meet you, nations will meet you, siblings will meet you, and parents will meet you.

Father, what kind of position are we in today? It is a painful reality to hear and see. Those who cannot experience this will find it regrettable. I have realized that if I do not run this path with my life, the world of love will block my way. At this time, when the sighs of grief are sweeping over our individuals and the world, please allow us to establish the standard of heart as an unchanging center with the principles of heaven, so that we can laugh at the world and the authority of the satanic world, and may we become sons and daughters who have completed the standard of heart of heaven, enjoying it together with heaven.

Today, being able to speak such words in this place is the last of my 40 years of life. I earnestly wish that this hour will be the occasion for a bright day to be granted to us tomorrow, and I pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. *

Words about Holy Salt and Separation
<Summary of the Words> Holy salt is like leaven. 
When you buy something, you must separate it, and when you come home from outside, it is principle to separate at the fence (at the gate). 
Do not give what has been separated to the satanic world. If unavoidable, give it with your left hand. 
Separation is done in the name of the Father, the Son, the Holy Spirit, and the True Parents. Sprinkle the holy salt in a cross (North-South, East-West order). 
When disposing of separated real estate, it is principle to obtain permission through the class, group, and regional levels. 
Our members must gradually occupy all lands as separated lands. * 
<Reference> 
April 11, 1960 (Monday), at the former headquarters church.

Just before the marriage ceremony held on the morning of April 11, the teacher began the work of holy salt by separating the venue with newly made holy salt.

79 
Holy salt means 
Holy salt is originally white salt. It is a conditional object that renews all things and distinguishes them as heavenly. 
Holy salt began to be used from April 11, 1960 (March 16 in the lunar calendar). It is separated by sprinkling holy salt in a cross on the separated objects. This is not used for food but only for separation, and in the future, it will be distributed to future members to use with the same intention. When it is about to run out, pour the "base" of holy salt in multiples of seven of the unit amount and pray with your heart. In this way, it can be supplemented for a long time and its function can be extended.

Before preaching, the teacher spends more time praying for the members than praying for the sermon. Father! I must lead these people up; how do I do it? Is it this or that? After gathering sincerity, he preaches according to the command of his heart.

As you get closer to your destination, the purpose and will grow larger, and I become smaller. As long as you have the heart that is smaller than yourself and larger than the will, everything will be resolved. 
As you get closer to the endpoint of providence, do not elevate yourself or be arrogant. You must have the heart that humbly approaches the greater, higher, and more magnificent will from a position of utter humility. 
Never lose hope. No relative object can bring you despair. Despair or disappointment is entirely subjective to oneself. 
What unfolds before you, any phenomenon or fact, is not the problem; the issue is your own mindset towards it. For example, even when looking at a bowl of rice, depending on whether the observer has the heart of a rich person or a poor person, that rice will have a different effect. 
When the teacher interacts with you, it is not about the success or failure of the work but about the emotional motivation behind it. In other words, whether it is self-centered or God-centered is what matters. If it aligns with what God has established from a heart-centered perspective, all problems will be resolved.

8)
The Significance of the Holy Ceremony
<Summary of the Words> Today's holy ceremony is God's hope and ideal. 
It is the holy ceremony that was to be fulfilled when Adam and Eve matured. It is truly a historical event that was within the heart of creation. One must realize that this ceremony is the first to occur since creation. The three disciples of Jesus should have shared life and death with their teacher. From now on, remember that your body is not your own. Live with the heart of being an offering. 
One man and one woman are the sons and daughters manifested as the substantial object of the incorporeal God. The man represents God's plus (+) nature, and the woman represents God's minus (-) nature. The ideal of creation is to separate God's nature into the duality of gender and then to synthesize and unify it into a form resembling God's original nature. 
One man and one woman each resemble God's singular nature. Therefore, the union of these two, one man and one woman, is the coming together of God's plus (+) and minus (-) natures. In other words, they become the harmonious entity that resembles God. Thus, the two human beings, that is, the couple, represent the entirety of God. 
By representing God's plus (+) nature, the man becomes the embodiment of the True Father, and by representing God's minus (-) nature, the woman becomes the embodiment of the True Mother. They are also each God's representatives. To love one another is to embrace the cosmos. This is a cosmic reunion. 
The husband is a being that represents many men; thus, he is a husband, a substitute for the father, and a substitute for the older brother. The wife represents many women; thus, she is a wife, a substitute for the mother, and a substitute for the older sister, so they must love and respect each other. *

Words for the Easter Memorial Service
<Summary of the Words> Today is the day we commemorate the resurrection of Jesus from the tomb 2,000 years ago. 
The purpose of God's restoration work is to achieve resurrection, and within that purpose of resurrection, all of creation is included. Above, there is heaven; below, there is earth and all humanity, and nothing is outside this realm. 
The path to resurrection that everyone must take
If humanity had not fallen, the term resurrection would not exist. A true human must feel that they are unworthy before heaven and earth. 
The path of resurrection is a path that all fallen humanity must take. The solution to resurrection is not in the heavenly throne, nor in the spiritual world, nor in any leader or scripture. It is also not found in today's Christianity itself. 
God's providence is a restoration providence. Our humanity, due to the fall, has not fulfilled the purpose of creation, so it must be recreated through the process of resurrection.
Today, we who have gathered here must look forward to the day of resurrection. Through the earth, on April 17, 1960 (Sunday), at the middle of the hillside behind Samcheong Park in Seoul.

86 Easter Memorial Service Message  
We must resurrect the heavenly (spiritual) world. We know that the basis of resurrection is in the heavenly realm, but that is not true. It is on this earth. This earth is the center. The basis and solution for resurrection are here on this earth. If resurrection does not occur on this earth, then the resurrection of the heavenly realm, the resurrection of humanity, the resurrection of all things, and the resurrection of the people in hell will remain mere nouns. Therefore, someone must first resurrect on this earth.  
In the spirit world, there are hell, the intermediate spirit world, paradise, and heaven. Until now, all those who have been faithful before heaven are in paradise. Jesus is also in paradise. In achieving the purpose of resurrection, the indirect destination is the spirit world, and the direct destination is the earth. The spirit world is the place to be resurrected, and the earth is the place that must be resurrected. Therefore, first,  
I have resurrected on this earth. I have concluded the purpose of resurrection.  
Only by being able to say this can we go to the heavenly kingdom. If such a person appears on this earth, everything on the ground cannot help but move. Many prophets and sages have longed for the day of participating in the first resurrection, and that day is when the purpose of resurrection is fulfilled.  
The heavenly realm is a place that manages the things of the earthly realm. What will be the center of this management in the future? We must manage the world centered on the personality of Jesus. When that happens, the era of managing with the words of Jesus will pass, and the era of sacrifice and service will also pass.  
Actions taken in the fallen world ultimately leave behind pain and sorrow, but we must transcend this and create a world where we can freely sing the heart of love with Jesus on the earth. To victoriously conclude the work of resurrection on the ground, we must first inherit and practice the heart of Jesus to liberate God. We must pass through the heart that can make God, the source of happiness, hope, freedom, and ideals, rejoice.  
Christians have looked at the Lord of the cross and have had faith until now. They have thought about it to the point of weariness. By crucifying Jesus, they have increased God's heart of pain and grief. The Jesus who carved wood in the house of Joseph was purer and more hopeful than the Jesus who suffered on the cross. Therefore, the cross is filled with the twists of tragedy.  
87  
We know that the Lord who suffered on the cross is the whole purpose of the Lord's coming, but how wonderful it would have been if Jesus had become one who devoted himself to heaven without suffering?  
The pure preaching of the gospel by Jesus had a good start. If we had accepted such a Jesus, there would have been no content in the Bible where Jesus rebuked. If there had been individuals or groups saying, "Master, please do not rebuke me," it would not be like this today.  
We thought that the Lord who wore a crown of thorns and bled from being pierced by a spear was all of the Lord. However, if we had believed in Jesus who did not suffer on the cross one hundred percent, how much more precious would that have been than believing in the Jesus who suffered on the cross? Heaven demanded that. However, everywhere Jesus went, there were arrows from Satan, and places torn apart due to despair arose. The pain God experienced until Jesus resurrected was much greater than Jesus' pain. We must understand this.  
Today, we are also required to have a pure heart of resurrection. The Father desires to meet a figure who has not received any wounds. However, we, born of Satan, have marks pierced by Satan's arrows, and the Father, who must see that, is filled with resentment and pain.  
We must open the door of our hearts.  
Therefore, we must long for and sing about the appearance of the living Jesus and celebrate Easter. Jesus is pleased to see this. History is also hoping for it. Heaven says,  
"Endure. Endure and sacrifice. Even if the body is torn and dies, do not receive wounds in the heart world and do not leave blemishes."  
Paradoxically, heaven desires a being whose heart and body have not been invaded by Satan, so at any time, whether young or old, one must not receive wounds in that heart. Heaven wishes for it to always be beautiful, precious, bright, and clean.  
88 Easter Memorial Service Message  
Until now, the prophets and sages have been infinitely sorrowful in body and heart. However, no one has yet mourned in heart. The sorrow of the heart world is still an unexplored field. We have been called as pioneers to pioneer this field.  
Therefore, we must overcome the three gates of the body's appeal, the heart's urging, and the heart's urging.  
You have been called as historical pioneers who can turn back history. This is not just words. Only by opening the door of the heart can faith appear, and God can freely walk among us. Therefore, first is the heart, second is the heart.  
We must pass through the door of the heart anyway. Without establishing the condition of having passed through the door of the heart, we cannot resurrect. Jesus could not enter the kingdom of heaven because he could not solve the problem of the heart. Therefore, the first is the heart, and the thousandth and ten-thousandth are also the heart. This door of the heart must be opened for the door of heaven to open. On the day the door of heaven opens, a person who has not received wounds in body, heart, and spirit can enter the kingdom of heaven. A person who replaces what Jesus must do without receiving wounds in body, heart, and spirit is a brother of Jesus. He can call Jesus brother or older brother. This is a privilege among privileges.  
The history of the past has been a history of fighting to seize external land and wealth. However, now is the era of fighting to seize the inner person and ideology. Because this internal battle has not yet been resolved, the door of heaven remains tightly closed. Only when the perfect being emerges will this battle be resolved, and the door of heaven will open. That is the opening of the heart. Therefore, the entire heavenly and earthly realm must achieve freedom and openness in the heart realm. The heavenly and earthly realms are groaning even now to establish connections in the heart.  
God created all things in the universe with connections of heart. Therefore, even a blade of grass is connected with heart. However, humanity has lost that connection due to the fall. If there is someone who can connect the connection of heavenly heart and earthly heart, he can solve anything in heaven and earth.  
History is a history of recreation. The history of recreation is to find one person.  
89  
Thus, until now, we have fought material-centered wars to seize the land, like the body of a person, and wars centered on ideologies to seize the mind, like space. In the future, there will be a heart-centered war that seizes the heart corresponding to the spirit world. We are placed in a historical burden to open our hearts and seek heaven.  
You, gathered here under the name of family, have come together to complete the resurrection, but have you been liberated from the fight to seize the body? Have you been liberated from the fight to seize ideology? If not, you have not resurrected. To be resurrected, you must possess the content of resurrection. By going through bodily resurrection and causing a resurrection of the heart, you will attain the value of beauty before the fall, that is, the original beauty. If this is accomplished on the ground, everything in heaven, earth, and all things will be resolved.  
If you do not feel a sense of explosive force pulling in all directions regarding the center of heaven, then the heart resurrection has not yet occurred. No matter what pain you are in, if there is no stronger shock of heart that can surpass that pain, you cannot participate in the first resurrection. There must be a strong action of heart that can feel heaven and earth, time and space all at once, and that can surpass the pain of hell's bottom for you to participate in the first resurrection.  
The main purpose of the restoration process—resurrection of body, heart, and spirit  
The main purpose of the restoration process we are facing today is to meet the Lord of the Second Advent. The mission of the Lord of the Second Advent is to restore the heart that was lost due to the fall. Therefore, we must not fail to raise a great history of resurrection regarding the one who comes to conquer the heart.  
The one who comes to connect God's heart directly to the earth is the Lord of the Second Advent. He comes to find the people living on the earth. We who have gathered here are a group selected from among countless humanity.  
In the spirit world, there are countless spirits. There is not a single thing that was created without passing through the connection of God's heart. Therefore, God is trying to save not only this earth but also millions of spirits in the heavenly realm. He wishes to move the world centered around us. Thus, we must understand God's heart that seeks to restore.  
The hearts of Adam and Eve, whom God created with great care, died due to the fall. It has been 6,000 years to resurrect that heart. Since the sons and daughters who were to take charge of heaven and earth have died, should they not be revived? God is longing for the dead children to come back to life. His will is to find and establish a complete Adam and Eve with a standard of heart and restore the entire world at once.  
Now, the whole world must establish a unified ideology. All materials are prepared, so we just need to work hard. We only need to move our bodies. In a free environment, we can do the errands as the angels did at the time of creation. We can offer all that we have. Thus, first, the body must be resurrected, second, the heart must be resurrected, and third, the spirit must be resurrected.  
To be resurrected as the sons of God, the body must be torn and ripped, but it must not fall and must establish the standard of victory to connect with God and the heart.  
God! Until now, the vertical history has been like this, so I will do it horizontally.  
Many may be able to do this, but not many can play the role of the cloth that contains God's heart.  
While we are in the world, there are many times we go to places that heaven does not want. Even if we go through such paths, we must advance to the door of the heart.  
To see a blade of grass or a flying bird and have the heart explode is to enter the stage of completing resurrection. Whether walking on the road, eating, or doing anything, there must be a heart that precedes that. Heaven looks for that, and because we cannot do so, it is saddened. If there is something felt in the heart, hold on tightly and look at it. If the heart is strong enough that it cannot let go even if told to, it can head towards heaven. If one is such a person, there is no problem.  
If the heart is stronger than the teacher's, it is okay to go anywhere. You must think of the restoration providence as soon as you open your eyes and become a valuable person who establishes the purpose of heaven in reality, striving to achieve the day of resurrection. The teacher also thinks of this as soon as he opens his eyes.  
Today, the issue is our hearts on this Easter. We must become people who produce valuable flavor in reality as heaven desires. Until now, there has been no one in heaven or on earth who has completed resurrection, and it is a matter for which we must bow our heads in gratitude that resurrection will occur from this poor nation on the Korean Peninsula. If there is someone who has achieved this standard, he is a person who cannot be exchanged for any amount of wealth. He appears to be someone who has lost everything, yet he is someone who possesses everything. He is a son and daughter who returns joy, happiness, and delight to the Father who comes holding the initiative of the heart. Therefore, we must be grafted into his world of heart.  
God is our Father, and the Lord is our bridegroom. Heaven has made us aware of longing, devotion to God, and loyalty. Now we must unify the attention with the heart of a father, the heart of a couple, and the heart of a ruler and subject. Under the name of that Father, there is nothing that cannot be forgiven, and no entanglements can arise. In the name of the bridegroom, there is nothing that cannot be yielded. When serving under one king, we cannot be disunited. This is the conclusion of heart resurrection.  
For 40 years, I have wished to say such words just once, and today, as I have done so, I hope you all consider this an infinite glory and keep it in mind. *

하나님의 최대의 소망은 무엇일까요? 그것은 바로 인간이 본연의 자리로 돌아가 하나님과 함께하는 것입니다. 인간이 하나님과의 관계를 회복하고, 그분의 뜻을 이루어가는 삶을 살기를 원하시는 것입니다. 

오늘 여러분은 어떤 선택을 하시겠습니까? 여러분의 삶이 하나님의 뜻에 부합하는 삶이 되기를 바랍니다. 하나님은 여러분의 선택을 기다리고 계십니다.
Those who cannot do so are coming out as stones of support, believing in heaven. The true loyal subjects, filial children, and virtuous women of heaven
