And if the child understands that heart, they will know everything with just one word from the parent.

The duty of a loyal subject

Today, we have heard many words. However, what can connect from one end to the other is not words but heart. 

Do you know what it means to say, "I am the Alpha and the Omega"? Is the Bible made up of Alpha and Omega? Each chapter of the 66 books from Genesis to Revelation is completely different; can they be Alpha and Omega? That is a statement made with the heart. The heart does not change. It simply exists eternally. This is the foundation of our life.

We must carry this heart and advance through the positions of the bride and groom to the positions of true sons and daughters, loyal subjects, and virtuous women. Once we enter such positions, no matter where we go in heaven and earth, that person will not starve to death. I have lived like this without a penny, but I have never gone hungry. Even when I was crowded in prison, someone would bring me food. You must understand that.

Everyone, after putting in all your strength, sweat, and tears in prayer, do not have the mindset of saying, "Oh Father, today I have made a prayer of grace." You should not think, "I have done enough now." If you do, grace will gradually disappear. Therefore, you must always reflect on yourself as a sinner and stand in a position where you feel the historical crimes. 

Those who boast of their own greatness cannot hold their heads up in front of those who come with good hearts, those who come with true hearts. God is the same. In front of those who put in all their sincerity and come with a heart of loyalty, God also bows His head. In front of a true loyal subject, even parents bow their heads. In front of a true bride, even the groom bows his head.

Everyone, do not say, "I believe and..." and boast. The person speaking here is not bragging. However, I am confident in facing the world of Satan. We Unification Church members must have the attitude of realizing our inadequacy even after offering sacrifices at the altar built on hope. That attitude is the attitude that the people of heaven should take. Even after putting in all our sincerity, those who do not have regret and realization, saying, "Oh, I wish I had done this differently," will be pushed aside. They cannot enter the deep world of God's heart. They cannot open the door of God's heart and move all the treasures of heaven and earth. God longs for sons and daughters who have such regret and realization to appear on this earth. Everyone, think about it. If God exists, would it be otherwise?

What is the highest purpose of God, who has sought for 6,000 years? After establishing the nation of heavenly sovereignty, it is to teach the people the duty of loyal subjects. This is God's wish. But everyone, go to the heavenly kingdom. There is no one there to teach you that this person is a loyal subject and how to go this way. They do not teach you that if you do this and that, you will surely become a loyal subject of heaven. They do not teach you that the nation that heaven wants to establish is this kind of nation and that the enemies must be subdued like this.

Have we received the teachings of loyal subjects today? Have we received the teachings that say, "This is how God's family should be, and to become true sons and daughters who can represent God, you must do this"? We have not received them. Furthermore, have you received the teachings of the bride and groom that say, "You must do this and that to be proclaimed before heaven and earth as my beloved bride"? We have not received them. Does the Bible teach such things? It does not.

If the path we must take is such a path, we must break through it without regard for life and death. If this is the fate of fallen humanity, what should we do? We cannot enjoy today with joy. We cannot be that kind of life. If we spend an hour enjoying ourselves, our descendants will clench their fists and strike the ground, fearing the judgment seat and lamenting. If you are concerned about that, you must avoid the comfortable position of today and strive to know where the heavenly heart is.

Therefore, we must understand the heart of Jesus, who was sent after 4,000 years of labor, the heart of Jesus who grew up as the son of a carpenter in Joseph's family, the heart of Jesus who was persecuted by the Pharisees during his three years of public life, and the heart of Jesus who was cornered by the Israelite people. Do you know the heart of Jesus? The one who sold Jesus was one of the disciples who followed Jesus for three years. You must understand that even though they lived and ate together, they became the betraying apostles who sold their master and the heart of Jesus who was betrayed.

The heart of God and Jesus

Today, the Christianity of the world is not a matter of revolution. It must be turned upside down. It must be fundamentally overturned. If it cannot be done through human ethics, it must be overturned by relying on heavenly ethics. We have arrived at an enormous time where we must put things back on the right track.

The heart of Jesus, who was chased, the heart of Jesus who cursed the fruitless fig tree while wandering in Bethany because he was hungry (Mark 11:12), the heart of Jesus who lamented, "I have a baptism to be baptized with, and how distressed I am until it is accomplished" (Luke 12:50), the heart of Jesus who prayed, "Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me" — do you know the heart of Jesus? Do you think he said such words with a smile? Absolutely not. You must understand that he said those words while suppressing his tears.

What kind of trial is it for Jesus, who was sent after 4,000 years of labor? Do you know the heart of Jesus who said, "Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites!" to those who were testing him? Do you understand? Do you think you can understand the life of Jesus, who moved with content that you cannot comprehend? Mary Magdalene poured perfume on the feet of the virgin Jesus and wiped them with her hair; how many of you publicly acknowledged that?

Oh, hallelujah, amen. Raise your hands if you praised him. It was a life of great suffering for Jesus.

Throughout history, you have only known Jesus as one who is revered, but you have not known the heart of Jesus who was trampled and chased, who was nailed to the cross, and who was accused of being a traitor to his nation. Jesus was called a traitor to his nation, a destroyer of social order, and a madman. Wasn't he? Then why did you come and go like that? Have you ever thought, "I wish I could have been the garment that Jesus wore, or at least heard one word he spoke alone"? Or, "If I could have been the cushion where Jesus could rest, I could have felt the inner heart of the weary Jesus"?

Have you ever thought about that? 

Peter, John, and James, who were less than a stick, less than a blade of grass, and less than a rock, did everything they could and then killed him, and now they are saying this and that... I feel like I cannot call Paul or Peter my teacher even if I go to the spirit world. When I meet them, I want to grab them by the collar and ask, "Why did you let Jesus be nailed to the cross?" If I say this, you may misunderstand.

However, history flows as it is, and heaven leads according to the law of justice.

You who are gathered here, do not listen to the words that say Jesus was swayed by the wind. Heaven sighed when it saw John the Baptist. Jesus asked, "Are you a reed shaken by the wind?" (Matthew 11:17). After 30 years of preparing in the wilderness with locusts and wild honey, is that all he amounted to? 

We are sinners beyond words. Even if we fill heaven and earth with tears and repent, we are sinners for whom there is no way to repent, and we cannot find a way to be forgiven. Yet, there is a way for such sinners to be forgiven, and that is God's providence of salvation, which has the heart of restoration.

Everyone, knowing this, you must now cling to God, who was rejected by the old Adam, and weep. Have you ever cried out, "My Father, where are you?" toward God, who looked upon the fallen family of Adam with deep sorrow? After 1,600 years, God raised Noah and made him build the ark with all his sincerity and effort, but due to Ham's mistake, he could not fulfill his purpose and was left in endless sorrow. Have you ever wept holding onto that God? After raising Moses from the royal palace and leading the chosen people of Israel to cross the Red Sea and into the wilderness, did you understand the heart of God, who suffered all kinds of humiliation to lead out the unfaithful people? After all the hardships, God wanted to bring them into the blessed land of Canaan, but did you understand the heart of God as He watched Moses collapse? Furthermore, after promising to send the Messiah, the historical subject of hope and providential purpose, through countless prophets over 4,000 years, He was killed. Did you understand the heart of God as He watched Jesus being killed?

The path to truly receiving God's blessing

The place you can go through the heart is heaven. Jesus is also in paradise. Do you know what paradise is? It is a waiting room. It is the waiting room for the heavenly train. It was the responsibility of Jesus, who came to this earth, to resolve the heart issues here, but he could not fulfill that responsibility and left, so he must come again to complete that responsibility. Only then can the door of paradise be opened. Only by opening the door of heaven can the world of Satan be subdued.

Those who have not completed the kingdom of the heart on earth cannot establish the kingdom of heaven in the spiritual realm. Those who have not found the eternal welfare of the heart on earth cannot find the eternal welfare in the spiritual realm. Have you found such a heart of welfare? You are all struggling like orphans without having found that welfare. Therefore, when viewed from the heart of God, your hearts have no position. Without a position, there is no value. How can a world have a relationship with a being of no value?

Thus, as true sons and daughters, as true loyal subjects, as true virtuous women, we must raise a group that can enjoy the ideology of life on behalf of the heart of heaven, and they must multiply the good sons and daughters on this earth. Was it to multiply the children of sin in the world of Satan that God blessed Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden? No. It was to multiply sons and daughters with the loyalty of a loyal subject, the devotion of true sons and daughters, and the virtue of virtuous women. God longs for the second loyal subjects and true sons and daughters to be born in that way. If such sons and daughters do not appear, this earth will forever belong to Satan.

Then why can the sons and daughters of the world of Satan not be proven by God as His eternal sons and daughters? It is because the emotional connection has not been completed. It is because there is no mutual understanding. This is the problem.

When you believe in Jesus and receive grace and pray before Him, you should feel a sense of whether you are inside your body or outside of it. You must experience a world of heart where you do not want to step away from that place forever. When you are embraced, you should feel like a father and a mother.

If you are a loyal subject, you must advance to a place where God can forget His dignity and embrace you, weeping. If there are loyal subjects who have triumphed over the realm of life and death, subduing the world of Satan and paving the way for God's victory, would God have the feeling that I am the king and you are the subject? God will forget His dignity, take your hand, weep with tears of joy, and say, "All of heaven and earth is yours. If you rejoice, I will also rejoice," and bless you. Only when such sons and daughters appear on this earth will the universe be turned upside down. If such a place arises on this earth, that place will become the center of the world in the future, and if such a nation arises, that nation will dominate the world in the future.

Unification Church members must establish the tradition of loyalty and filial piety

However, as mentioned earlier, heaven first drives such a nation into a place of sorrow. It drives them into a place of suffering. It puts them into a place of historical adversity. Why? Because God carries all the burdens of suffering and comes to seek them. Therefore, the place where global suffering is concentrated will be the place to untie God's burden of suffering and the place to pioneer a new foundation.

Today, although the Korean people are said to be the most pitiful nation in the world, I have the greatest hope for the Korean people. Although the democratic world and the communist world are in confrontation, this nation is not a pitiful nation. Just wait a few years. The Korean people are absolutely not a pitiful nation. If there is a heavenly movement, this nation will survive. History is the history of this nation, and the world will become the world of this nation. This is not my word. It is because it has become that way that I say so. The providence of restoration that follows history has been carried out from the back alleys of sorrow. From there, the foundation of joy has been established, and the way has been paved.

That is why Korea is currently a problem in the world.
The issue of the Christian community is becoming a problem. In the future, the Unification Church will emerge as a global issue. This is not a boast. Just wait and see. Those who pray will know. Those who are spiritually enlightened will testify. If we do not act, we will be caught by heavenly law. Therefore, everyone gathered here must be firmly prepared for what lies ahead. We cannot afford to be complacent. We must have the conviction that no matter what persecution we face, we will not let it become a problem. Just one thing: even if we fall, we must establish the tradition of loyalty and filial piety that we want to build. If we establish the traditions of loyal sons and daughters, virtuous men and women, and filial sons and daughters, the Unification Church will fulfill its mission.

In establishing traditions, we must create an official tradition that can be explained as "if you do this, this will happen," rather than "it could be this way." Humanity, which wanders in longing for the heart, must pass through the door of this tradition anyway. No matter how much they betray or oppose, they cannot avoid passing through this door. The person speaking here believes this. And they are practicing it. Everyone gathered here also acknowledges this. If you cannot acknowledge this, then please leave. If you think it is a lie, then go. You are a hindrance.

We must shed tears. If that heart is not felt, we must shed tears. If that heart is not felt, we must pray all night. We must pray even while fasting. Only those who carry such a heart will achieve the final victory and remain in the final judgment. If you become such people, God will prepare a place of rest through you, and the world will move because of you. If you feel and understand this, you must now have something to say before the 2.8 billion people of humanity.

To become a loyal servant of heaven, we must repay the enemies of heaven. To be a filial child, we cannot leave the enemies of our parents; we must eliminate the enemies. The same goes for virtuous women. Unless we prepare ourselves to fight with the determination to stake our eternal lives until the day we repay these enemies, you will not be able to cross the sorrowful peak of corruption. Only by crossing this peak will God finally release all the sorrowful hearts and bless you, saying, "O loyal servant, O filial child, O virtuous woman," and He will be able to rest. Until the standard of heart is resolved, there can be no rest.

Knowing this, I hope you can feel how precious each of you gathered here this evening is.

<Prayer> Father, we acknowledge that we are unworthy to call You Father. What is the greatest hope of God's blessing? There are many kinds of fathers, including others' fathers, stepfathers, and even the fathers of enemies. We do not wish for such fathers; we desire the true Father.

If we can communicate with the heart of that Father, we know that many prayers are not necessary. When we say "Father," that is everything; it is enough for all hearts to connect. In that place, we can look upon all creation with a heart of gratitude and reverence, embracing it at the intersection of joy and sorrow.

We have come to realize how amazing it is to call You Father. However, we pray that we may not be children who merely call Your name but rather children who hold onto the Father we have felt in our hearts.

What kind of connection do we have that we gather here to speak and listen? Because we cannot stop the footsteps of our sorrowful journey of restoration, we are gathered here today to hear these words. Let us not forget that this is not something we have wished for but is due to the infinite efforts of heaven working behind the scenes.

We understand that our hearts do not move from our own creative consciousness but always move from a passive standpoint. If we do not move in this way, we cannot be at ease. We have come to this place to avoid a state of discomfort, and we know that it is because heaven has extended a loving hand to us even in suffering.

The children of Yours gathered here today have already made up their minds. We have gathered here to offer our red hearts to You, Father, without expecting any reward or compensation, wishing only to fulfill our loyalty to You.

Please take this heart and boast of it to the whole world, and do as You wish. We earnestly hope and wish to be able to do so.

There are those who could not attend this evening, and many of Your children who are shedding tears in lonely places, calling out to You. They are pitiful beings, so please protect them. We earnestly ask that all of us become companions of joy who can fill the footsteps of sorrow left at the end and be those who can hold onto Your heart and comfort You.

We entrust everything to You, so please take charge. We earnestly ask for Your blessing so that the words we have shared today may be of help to their lives, and we pray in Your name. Amen.

<Happy Groups>
Ecclesiastes 7:23-29
<Prayer> Please be with us in this time You have allowed, Father. At this time when heaven and earth cannot find their center and are trying to decide life and death, Father, please bless us.

Humans have lost the center of their hearts, the center of their minds, and the center of their bodies, and they have lost the center of their lives, society, nation, world, and heavenly principles. Father, please let us feel how sorrowful we are at this time.

How pitiful are the humans who are struggling to live while having lost everything? They may boast of having something, but that too is something they must lose. They sing of their individual rights and boast of their glory, but that too must be lost. Humans acknowledge that their value is infinitely great in their hearts, but they are placed in a miserable position where they must live longing for that value while having lost their true worth. We are such beings, and Father, You know us very well.

You have worked hard to find what has been lost, and we have also worked hard. We have struggled to find the lost words, but we have not been able to find them. We have struggled to find the lost people, but we have not been able to find them. Because we could not find that one person, we could not find the standard of one body, one mind, and one heart. Therefore, we could not find a family that could live with God, and because we could not find such a family, society, nation, and world have gone astray, becoming a world that only accelerates Your sorrow. Father, how can we not lament this?

My Father, how sorrowful You must have been! My Father, how sad You must have been! My Father, how lamentable You must have been! We, Your unworthy children, should gather to take away a part of Your worries, to alleviate Your sorrow, and to add joy, yet today we find ourselves in a pitiful position that adds sorrow to You. Please forgive us.

You are love and the embodiment of glory and patience. Knowing that You bear all the good and bad names on this earth, we are sad because of You, happy because of You, troubled because of You, and joyful because of You. There is no one on this earth who knows the sorrow of the Father, who should be our friend and parent in such a position. There are no true filial sons or true filial daughters who know that sorrow of the Father.

If there is sadness, we realize that there is no greater sadness than this, and if there is something to lament, we realize that there is no greater fact to lament than this. We have gathered to become friends of Your sorrow and to hold onto Your lonely heart, shedding tears together and enduring pain together, so please visit us at this time.

Who are we looking to as we gather? Father! Please do not let us be those who gather looking to any person, nor let us be those who gather out of longing for someone. We have come seeking You, and with a heart that desires to be close to You, to approach the heavenly throne, we have come with that one heart, and having moved our steps to this place of longing, we earnestly hope and wish for Your blessing and presence here.

Now, what shall I say? Until this day and time, I have spoken many words. I know that I must take responsibility for that, so Father, please be with us here. As the time of heaven approaches, the people on this earth do not know that I am in a position where I cannot help but speak. Please let Your children gathered here truly come to know this fact. 

Let us live with the words, practice with the words, and harmonize with the words so that we can establish a standard of overall life. We have gathered not for anything in this world. We have gathered to give our utmost sincerity and loyalty to bring closer the kingdom of Your glory, and to comfort the Father who has crossed over the peak of sorrow, so please do not let us stand in the position of children who are indebted again at this time. 

Let us be heavenly children who can call You my Father with joyful faces and who can call You my Father with a united heart and body, filled with earnestness. 

This alone is Your wish, and this alone is Your will, so Father, please allow this time to be a time of grace. Please let this time be one where we can meet You, wipe away our tears of sorrow, and overflow with joy to sing of gratitude and glory. We earnestly ask that this time may be one where we can step forward as the embodiment of the words You have given and as representatives of all creation, making a resolution and determination.

We earnestly ask that the sincere heart to draw closer to You through the gifts You give and the words You allow may be allowed to revive in each of our hearts at this time, and we pray all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Words> Today, I will speak on the topic of "Happy Groups."

The happy ones on this earth usually refer to those who possess something that others do not. People say that those who have joy that others do not have are happy people. If we possess something that we want to boast about in front of any being or creature, we can say that we are happy people.

Today, countless humans hope to be happy. The reason you have come here today is for happiness beyond what you are currently living. In other words, you have come to seek a connection with the world of heart and emotion beyond everyday happiness. This is acknowledged by all. And the desire to be happy forever, beyond tomorrow, beyond the day after tomorrow, beyond this year, and beyond next year, is the desire of humanity as we are born and live on this earth.

Unhappy humans
If God exists, what does He wish for His creations? He desires that the created beings be together where God is, and that if God is happy, the created beings should also be happy. From this perspective, we can think that all creatures were created.

We do not know what kind of connection we have, but we were born on this earth. Borrowing the term of religion, we can simply say that we are created beings. If we are creatures, there must be an absolute being who created us, and we call Him God.

However, what kind of relationship do we humans, who have been created by God, have with Him that today’s humans are in such a state? Did God create us imperfectly, or is the God who created us imperfect? This is a dilemma that contemporary humans may have.

It is said that God is the supreme and ultimate being. To say He is the supreme and ultimate being, it must encompass all the ideal elements of our lives. Moreover, it must possess the content that can fully satisfy the emotions of knowledge, emotion, and will that flow from the human heart. Only then can God be our absolute subject and the center of absolute purpose and exist as a reality. However, there is a condition that prevents humans from being connected to the existence of the supreme and ultimate being, and that condition is called evil, and the emergence of that condition is called the fall.

Among all the creations of God, there is nothing that exists without purpose. Even the smallest microorganisms, like bacteria, are meant to exist for some purpose. From the moment we were born of our parents' blood, even if we do not know it, we must recognize that we exist as a material to fulfill the purpose of the great heavenly principles.

As a material for some purpose, when the time comes to unite with the reality of that purpose, then and only then will that material fully demonstrate its value, and at that time, it can fulfill its requirements and its intended purpose. Similarly, for humans, there must come a time when we can finally say we are happy.

However, today we have laid bare our hearts and emotions, and when we analyze any aspect of life in detail, happiness may exist as a concept, but we do not possess anything to boast about as being happy. Not only do we lack something to boast about as being happy, but we also lack that precious something that others can see as happiness.

God must have established the purpose of the great universe and created all creatures, but if humans, after achieving that purpose, still experience sorrow, then I do not want such a creation. If achieving the purpose of creation involves suffering, everyone would dislike it. Therefore, even if there are sad and painful things after the purpose of creation is fulfilled, we cannot call them sorrow and pain. Rather, they may become materials that can stimulate joy and elements that can form life, but they cannot be elements that dominate life and violate the joy of happiness.

When we consider that there is not a single person in such a position on this earth, we can conclude that all people living on this earth are unhappy. When we think about being placed in such a position, we may feel that we have something, but in reality, we possess nothing. We may be boasting of ourselves, but we have nothing to boast about.

Even if I have life, that life cannot become a material for the ideals of the great universe or the world of happiness. Even if I have the character I have formed and the ideals I possess, and whatever I may boast about, because they have no relation to the ideals of the great universe, we cannot help but be unhappy.
What Humans Have Lost
We have all lost. We are worthless beings who cannot establish ourselves in this world. Therefore, what is the end of our hope as we seek happiness? It is to find what we have lost. There may be goodness in my heart, but there is no ultimate goodness. There may be love, but there is no ultimate love. There may be truth, but there is no ultimate truth. If we had the ultimate truth, no matter where we stayed or in what environment, we would be welcomed and liked. However, when we see that this is not the case, it shows that while I have the elements that can allow me to be good, I am not the embodiment of goodness, and while I have the elements that can allow me to be happy, I am not truly happy. We have all lost. What have we lost when viewed from a central perspective? We have lost everything when viewed in light of eternal ultimate happiness. This is something you must understand.

Look. The creatures that should know that the Creator, God, exists do not know. If humans, born with the Creator's intention, are to connect with that Creator, they must communicate through heart and intention. But what are you centered around? This lump of flesh? No. If this lump of flesh were connected to God, the subject of happiness, it should be satisfied, but it is not. The heart is not satisfied. The mind is not satisfied. We have all lost. From this perspective, humans have lost the essence and are struggling with an empty shell. We must understand that those who have strived to solve this problem are the people who walk the path of virtue and the enlightened sages.

Happy People
So, what have humans lost? First and foremost, we have lost God. Losing God is the greatest event among what we have lost. If there is a Master who has come to this world, and humans have lost that Master, then from that moment, humans become rebels before that Master. Humans should have the original Master, who can have a deep emotional connection, but they have lost Him. To fail to serve Him due to this loss is an act that cannot be accepted before the heavenly principles.

Do you know that God is somewhere in your heart, your cells, your emotions? You do not know. You may recognize it conceptually, but you are not in a position where you can emotionally recognize that God is here, that God is inherent among us. If there is sadness on this earth, what is the saddest thing among sad things? It is losing God. And what is the most painful thing? It is wanting to meet God but being unable to do so. It is not the pain of being beaten or despised. The true pain is not being able to meet the One you long for, miss, and want to see. That is sadness, that is pain, that is injustice. There is nothing more wronged than being unable to meet someone you can meet. You must have experienced this in your life journey.

Until now, humans have been sad, have suffered, and have walked a history of injustice, but those experiences are not meant to make humans feel sadness, pain, or injustice. They are meant to allow humans, who have lost their essence and their Master, to inherit God's sadness, pain, and injustice.

So, where does the origin of pain and sadness lie? Beyond historical origins, where does the principled origin lie? If you trace it back, the cause lies in losing God.

Therefore, although one may not know it well, deep in their heart, there is a connection to the creative touch of God, who created humans and all things. That connection transcends my body and environment, guiding us toward a holistic goal. Because of this, in the past, people were scattered and divided, but now they are gradually aiming toward a place where their hearts can be joyful. Thus, this world is being organized into a world of ideals.

When that world of ideals comes, the heart will settle. As the heart settles, the voice that cries out, "I am infinitely joyful," will erupt from within you and resonate throughout the universe. On that day, even if one is confined in a prison and in a place of suffering, a shout of happiness will burst forth. Such events must manifest in the course of history. That is why all religions say to willingly accept suffering. Every religion does. They say to gladly accept sadness. In doing so, they bring forth the world of the heart. Everything has been brought under the dominion of that world of the heart. Therefore, we must recognize that the time has come to gather everything and charge directly toward the original world of the heart. We must understand that the time has come when heaven and earth must unite as one.

We wish to be happy people. What must we do first to become happy? We must find what we have lost. First and foremost, we must find God. If there is a place where we can find the God we have lost, we must run toward that place, sacrificing everything.

As humans fell, they lost God, and at the same time, what else did they lose? They lost God's hope. What is God's hope? After creating the universe, God established Adam and Eve as the lords of all things and blessed them to be fruitful and multiply and to govern all creation. It was God's hope for humans to fulfill this blessing. On the day humans fulfill this blessing (God's desire), God becomes the Father of Adam and Eve, and Adam and Eve become His sons and daughters. Being God's sons and daughters is not a fictitious title. If it were fictitious, everything in Christianity would be a lie.

God's Will Regarding Adam and Eve
God created young Adam and Eve and hoped they would grow up to govern all creation. He did not want them to govern with words, but with love centered on His heart. That is why God wanted Adam to regard Eve as his bone of bones and flesh of his flesh, approaching her with a loving heart. He did not want Eve to serve Adam as an ignorant younger sister, but to regard Adam as the bridegroom and the body that replaces the father, serving him with a heart of love.

God, who hoped for such a time, wanted Adam and Eve to know that Adam is my eternal husband and Eve is my eternal bride. This is the Father's desire. He created them to govern this great nature as true parents who can fulfill the true love of God.

All things also wish to be governed in this way. In Romans 8, it is said that due to the fall of man, there arose groaning in heaven, groaning in humanity, and groaning in all creation. Because of humans... All things were created to be governed by the hands of Adam and Eve, who became true parents through true love, but Adam and Eve fell and could not enter that position. This is the fall. Therefore, today, while many people live in this world, is there anyone who approaches God with a heartfelt longing, calling Him Father? There is not. Have you ever thought that there might be such a person? There is not.

There has been no one on this earth who has called God Father from a position that goes beyond Adam and Eve before the fall, saying, "God! Is Your heart not like this? Is Your desired heart not like this?" There has been no one who could think that such a person existed. God desired that Adam and Eve, who were to fulfill God's hope and blessing, would come before Him and say, "Father! My Father!" However, God has never met such a true ancestor of humanity. He has not met such a person among their descendants. There is none.

The Father that believers today call upon is merely a nominal Father, a Father in name only. He is not the Father called from a place where the heart melts. There is no one who calls upon the Father from such a place. That is why God has come seeking such a person. He has come to reveal His position, His value, and His relationship with humanity. Thus, the 6,000 years of history have been a struggle to inform fallen humans that they are in a father-son relationship with Him. It is nothing else.

You speak of crowns of righteousness and other crowns, but I do not desire those. Jesus is not coming to do other things on this earth. He is coming to rule heaven and earth. The Jesus who comes in the end is a universal Jesus. The end is the time when Jesus comes to save sons and daughters who can be proud anywhere in heaven and earth. 
You cannot lead those who have died well in faith on this earth to God and say, "God, these are the sons and daughters who have believed well on the earth and have come to paradise. Please love them." While they may be proud within the realm of paradise, they cannot be proud within the overall heavenly ideology centered on the heavenly throne. In the era of the coming Jesus, Jesus Himself will go to the heavenly throne and say, "Father, here is a son who can be proud and loved by You, so please bless him as the great victor over all heaven and earth." You must become such sons and daughters. That is the goal that Jesus hopes for, and it is the goal that God hopes for. 
Today, in Christianity, people think that becoming a pastor is the highest position, but it is not. You must be able to face the national Lord beyond being a pastor. To move a church or a social organization, you must embody the national heart of Jesus. To become a leader who can represent all of Christianity, you must welcome the Jesus who comes globally. 
If you do not do that and continue in the old ways, Christianity will break apart. If the Lord comes in the future, He must be the main character who can govern heaven and earth and also be a son who can govern the heart of God. Do you understand what that means? It means you must be qualified to govern not only heaven and earth but also the heart of God. Such a qualified person is the Lord who is coming again. Know clearly that Jesus will return as such a main character. Only then will God be able to say, "Okay, you take care of all things in this world." After that, God will be able to rest. Isn't that logical? If you cannot establish a standard for resting on this earth, the ultimate resting place of history will not be achieved. 
In other words, we must liberate Jesus and God. Everyone, this is an enormous statement. Those who are here for the first time may call this heresy. That is fine. Why must we liberate Jesus? Jesus is still praying in paradise, so we must let Him cease that prayer.
Why should I liberate you? It is because God has become one who sheds blood and sweat and groans to save us, and thus we must be liberated. This is because He has not found His sons and daughters. It is not because something is lacking. It is not because heaven and earth are lacking. God has embraced the eternal ideal of creation, established the ideal of the whole, and blessed His sons and daughters, but a standard that can allow us to rest centered on our true ancestors has not been concluded. Therefore, in history, the axis of heaven's providence must be established. On the day this axis is placed in heaven and earth, the world will move faster toward the purpose of goodness, the more chaos there is.

Today, the Republic of Korea seems to be in turmoil and complexity, as if nothing is working, but the world is mobilized here. Just wait and see. It may seem like we are breaking apart internally, but the world is coming in. We are becoming more united. Those with a purpose must think carefully at this time.

Where does heavenly fortune flow? Those who move in the direction of heavenly fortune become loyal subjects, and there is no one who has moved against the direction of heavenly fortune who is not a traitor. The same goes for providence. Loyal subjects die for justice and the whole, while traitors die for themselves. That is the difference. We must die for the whole.

If a person possesses something precious, they should not just keep it to themselves. They must rejoice. They should rejoice together with the one who gave it to them. Only then can the giver also rejoice. If the giver has more, they should be able to say they want to give even more because they are so joyful. If one receives something worth hundreds of millions but only rejoices as if it were worth a few hundred thousand, it will be taken away. If you have received something precious, you must rejoice accordingly. A person whose heart overflows with such feelings is a happy person.

This joy is not a momentary joy. For those who wander in search of such things, for those with such a conscience, there is a desire to give and give again. They want to boast and boast again.

"Wow! This is truly good, wow! This is truly precious." For those who say this, they want to give everything, even at the cost of losing what is truly precious in the world. When you receive that precious thing, your heart must overflow with joy, and then you will think, "Now, pain is no problem." Who can take this joy away? If you rejoice in that way, then that joy is not just for the individual; it belongs to all people. A person who wants to boast, who wants to give, and who can rejoice even more when they see someone receiving is a happy person. Despite such principles, most humans claim that what is precious is theirs.

Those who say, "This is mine, and no one can touch it," are betrayers of heaven's providence. The fate of heaven and earth will strike those who go in that direction.

The responsibility of those who possess something precious
That is why we are told to be good. Goodness is infinitely precious. If you possess something precious, you should rejoice and then give it with a joyful heart. God is love. That is why God, even after losing His only begotten Son, says He will give more, forgetting His own difficulties. This is God's heart. You who must possess God, in order to have the content and elements of happiness, must rejoice, saying, "I have something precious." You must be grateful, saying, "The whole universe is looking for such a thing, and I have made Him mine!"

However, if you have made Him yours but feel the fear and threat of losing Him, then you have not yet truly possessed Him. But if you possess God, no one can take Him away. Why? Because He has become one with your body. Originally, God is the essence, and I am the body. That is why Jesus said, "I am the vine, and you are the branches" (John 15:5). Because we are one tree, as long as He is alive, I am also alive, and when He rejoices, I rejoice, and when He wants to give forever, I also want to give forever.

However, no matter how precious a thing you have, as long as you are in a position of fear of losing it, that is impossible. That is why Jesus said that the kingdom of heaven is within your heart, and "You will know that I am in the Father, and the Father is in me" (John 14:20). We must establish a bond of heart that is as strong as iron with God. Then, it is like using the same pocket of heart, so when God wants to jump out, everything will jump out. On the day the whole world becomes like that, nothing can be taken away.

The protagonists of the new era
If we closely observe the historical path, the Old Testament era was the era of offering material sacrifices, and the New Testament era is the era of offering body and heart as sacrifices. Jesus is the one who represented God's body and heart, thus being the ideal counterpart of God. Until now, you have known that the Holy Spirit gives grace, right? The Holy Spirit is the one who offers the body as a sacrifice. When this body sacrifice is completed, the bridegroom, Jesus, will also offer the heart as a sacrifice. The issue of heart arises in the place where the father and mother are united. In the past, material sacrifices were offered. Now, Christianity is a religion that offers body and heart as sacrifices centered on the Holy Spirit and Jesus. That is why it is said, "Love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, with all your mind, and with all your strength" (Mark 12:30). Thus, the sacrament of will is relative, isn't it?

Now, what will happen in the future? The era of material sacrifices and the era of body and heart sacrifices will pass, and ultimately, the era of heart sacrifices will come. It will be a time when one cannot live without longing for the Lord. With a heart that cannot live without longing for the Lord, when you go to the place where He dies, you must have a heart that can go there too. You must pass through the era of heart sacrifices. Why? Because humanity has fallen. Having betrayed the bond of heart, losing both heart and body, and losing all worldly matters, we must carry all of that in one body and restore it.

Because we are going through such a historical path, in finding the last elements of happiness that you have lost, you must become one with Him in heart and become one. When the heart becomes one, the historical distance is not a problem, the temporal distance is not a problem, and the spatial distance is not a problem. No matter where you go, it is always within that heart. Thus, we must become one in heart with heaven. When heaven is sad, I must also be sad, and when heaven is joyful, I must also become a participant who can rejoice. At the same time as becoming a participant on earth, when we go to heaven, we must also be a participant there. We must be participants in happiness. When Jesus is sad, I must be sad, and when He is joyful, I must be joyful, and when He is in anguish, I must be a participant who also feels anguish. Through that standard, in the end, we must want to give infinitely and want to boast infinitely. When that happens, centered on me, you will establish a relative relationship with all things, and through the affection with all things, you will relate to heaven.

You will have the three objects: heaven and heart, heart and body, body and all things. Only when this is established can you dominate Satan on earth and stand as victorious sons and daughters who have passed through the principles of heaven and earth. Such a person is the embodiment of God. If you are a man, you are the embodiment of the True Father, and if you are a woman, you are the embodiment of the True Mother. Who can sever such a bond? Even if countless Satans come, they cannot sever it. No matter how much someone says, "You are the son of someone," or "That person is not your mother," even if they beat, stab, or kill, that bond will not be severed.

Even if there is greater suffering, you must establish a relationship of unity with God and the bond of father and son. Only those who have such certain and empirical content, experiential facts will become the protagonists of the new era that is to come. Such a person will surely be able to pass through the process of judgment based on justice and will be able to live a happy life in a world of peace centered on love.

The fallen human being must abandon all notions of ownership.

It tells us to deny the ideologies and attentions of the world, to deny familial environments, and to deny individuals. Furthermore, it teaches us to deny our hearts and even our feelings. 
Why is that? What is the purpose? It is because God can only love what is not fallen. He cannot tolerate anything that has a connection with the elements of the fall. He tells us to deny in order to move us to the original world that is not fallen. 
If humans had not fallen, the whole world would be ours, and God would be ours. However, due to the fall, we lost the qualification to possess, so we must abandon everything we have. 
The visible world is not our world, and all created things are not ours. All of this belongs to God, and we must return it to God. From that position, we aim to reestablish a relationship with God and, after being reborn, to be placed in a position to govern all creation, which is the purpose of salvation. 
What is the most important thing for us to go through this process? It is the heart. The issue is where to set the standard of my heart. Everything I see, hear, and take joy in is not mine; it belongs to the realm of Satan. Humans have struggled until today to bring all of this into the heavenly realm. This is the purpose of history, the purpose of heavenly providence, and the purpose of creation. 

The heart of God can be felt through all things.

Children who can comfort God

Do you know what it means to be close to God? It is the place of repentance. However, upon closer examination, there is no need to ask for forgiveness for what sins you have committed. If you repent for not knowing the heart of the Father, you can be forgiven. 

A child who spends all of their parent's money and does all sorts of things commits a greater sin than hurting the heart of a father who loves them. There is no greater sin than that. Therefore, if there is a child who weeps, saying, "Father, this is something that can be here today and gone tomorrow, but how can I be forgiven for hurting your heart?" that father will say, "Okay, okay," and forgive them. That is how it is. Even fallen parents are like that, and God is the same. 

People go to church and pray, saying, "What sins have I committed? I repent, so please forgive me." However, more than that, they must say, "Please forgive me for the sin of violating the principles of heaven, for violating the connection between heaven and humanity, for destroying the connection between humanity and all things, and for the sins committed in the realm of the heart." 

By repenting in this way, if they are forgiven and recognized by the Father, then everything will be resolved. Heaven seeks such repentant people. It is true; it is true. 

To those who connect through the heart, all things in the world become theirs. <Word> The title I wish to think about with you today is "The Coming Father." I will briefly reflect on the title "The Coming Father." 

God who seeks to resolve the sorrow of the universe 
You know that the world you live in is not a world where you can sing of happiness forever. In society and family, and even when looking at oneself, we are vividly experiencing the sighs that remain in our bodies and hearts. 

Moreover, we often feel threatened in our lives and feel threatened in our daily lives, and we frequently find ourselves trapped in circumstances where we cannot move this way or that. However, even in such environments, in one corner of our hearts, we are fighting without losing hope to reject this self. 

When the heart desires to rejoice and urges the body to move toward something, if the body cannot go to that place and cannot take those steps, there can be no greater misfortune than this, and there can be no greater betrayal of the heart. 

When we think that this struggle does not end for a day or two, but continues throughout life and history, it becomes an important issue of how to resolve my current self. If I can set a victorious standard that can be recognized before all people by taking on this issue and resolving it, a new history, a new era, new happiness, and new joy will begin from me. Everything must be resolved from me. We must first recognize that this historical duty is imposed on each of us living on this earth. 

Humans who have brought sorrow to God 
If there is an absolute God who urges people's hearts to go toward some destination and gives them shock, what is it that God desires? You seek to solve not only your own problems but also the problems of this world, the created world, and all matters of heaven and earth. 

While we live with pain and sorrow, we can blame or vent our frustrations on friends, brothers, or family. We have such counterparts. However, we must feel once again that God, who has never had such a counterpart, harbors great sorrow and pain. 

There is a vast difference between the appearance of humans fighting to avoid their own pain and the appearance of God fighting to resolve the pain of the world. Even if I have worries and pains that seem to burst in my chest, those are personal pains. No matter how great that pain may be, we must understand that it cannot be compared to God's pain. 

Then, did God originally create humans in this way? Did God create all things to sweep them into sorrow and pain? No. Originally, He created them to feel joy. He created them to have a joyful heart and a happy spirit. 

Therefore, in God's eyes, there should be joy when He looks at all creation. However, today, when He looks at this earth, can God look at all things with a joyful heart? Can He look at humans with a joyful heart? It is not so. 

After creating all things in six days, on the sixth day, God created humans with a joyful heart. The ancestors of humanity, created in His image, were extremely beautiful beings, extremely precious beings, extremely proud beings, extremely joyful beings, extremely glorious beings, and beings He wanted to love. 

However, when you delve into the depths of your heart or examine each cell that makes up your body, is there anything there that can make God rejoice, that can make God happy, that can make God bless all things? There is none. 

God created all things to add joy and to continuously stimulate joy. He did not create them for momentary joy, but to feel the deep stimulation of joy and happiness every time He encounters His creations, pouring out the utmost heart. 

In this way, humans, created as the embodiment of God's entire heart, capable of replacing the joy of the entire creation, have been shattered. As a result, the created world, which was made for God's joy, has turned into a world of sorrow and pain, and Adam and Eve, who were the embodiment of joy and hope, were expelled from the Garden of Eden. Being a group expelled from before God, they must naturally suffer. They must naturally experience sorrow. They must suffer as a consequence of being traitors who abandoned the heavenly principle. 

Salvation through the heart 
Then, there must be a destination of joy that can reach us, who have betrayed God, and a method to remove all sorrow. This is what humanity, including you and me, has been searching for until today. 

We must find the original world where we can sing of joy, the original destination. We must also know the method to untangle all the pains of darkness that are entangled around us. Because we have not found that destination and did not know the method to remove the sighs of darkness and gloom, humanity has struggled in sighs, despair, and pain throughout thousands of years of history. 

Here, we must understand one thing: what is the limit of the pain, sorrow, and power of darkness that humans are experiencing? It is up to the brink of death, up to the brink of death. 

Now, even if the gateway of pain blocks our way toward that destination, we must become those who push through it, disregarding death. Such people can find any hope of the times or historical hope. Until we are willing to risk our lives and confront, God will not move. We must clearly understand that we are in such a position. 

God has not abandoned humans in such a position until now and has worked hard to bring them back to the world where only happiness exists. The purpose of salvation is to return to that world. Heaven is a secondary issue. Even if we live in pain on this earth, we must be able to swallow that pain and digest it into joy to go to heaven. Those who cannot do so absolutely cannot go to heaven. They cannot go. 

Do you believe you will go to heaven? Then let’s see. The Israelite people, who were set apart for 4,000 years centered on the will, how well did they believe? From Abraham through Moses until the coming of Jesus, for 2,000 years, how well did they keep the law established by Moses? A group that believed so well could never have imagined betraying Jesus, who came as the Prince of Faith. When they adorned the high priests and entered the atonement place, it seemed as if they were representing God and embodying faith, yet such people became enemies before Jesus. 

Where did the Israelites, who believed so well, go? We must recognize that their faithfulness was higher than the faithfulness of the believers who now believe in Jesus on this earth. The standard of salvation does not lie in how much one believes. It lies in how the heart is after believing. Can one go to heaven while harboring the mindset of a robber, the mindset of a thief, or the mindset of a murderer? Salvation does not work that way. From where does salvation begin? Salvation begins from the foundation, from the root. The root is the heart. That is why salvation begins from the heart. 

If there is a teacher guiding someone to become a person of character, that teacher must first conquer the heart of the disciple. Only then can the heart be led in a direction where it can develop. Before that, the disciple cannot be made into a person of character. A person cannot be made responsible with a complete character. 

Why does God want to save humans? What will He do after saving them? The purpose of salvation is for God to be pleased. God has been carrying out the providence of salvation to restore the original joy He had when creating all things. 

We must be saved from our own hearts, from our hearts. Therefore, God has been moving through the history of humanity, protecting the path of the heart, guiding the path of the heart, and stirring the hearts of humans. That is what God has done. 

The heart of humans should have become the house of God and Jesus 
Has God only been disappointed and cried after looking at the creation He made for 6,000 years? No. Jesus, who said, "It is finished" on the cross, did not just rest from that day. He is praying. What has He finished? Prayer is only necessary for the completion of purpose. 

When Jesus walked with the twelve apostles during His three years of public ministry, what was in His heart for those apostles? He did not want them to follow Him for the sake of food. That heart desired a heart in which Jesus could dwell. To host Jesus, their hearts must become the house of Jesus. If their hearts had become the house of Jesus, He would not have had to die. 

If Jesus had work to do, they should have said, "Lord, I will work in Your place," and if Jesus had to suffer, they should have said, "I will suffer in Your place," and if Jesus had to grieve, they should have said, "I will grieve in Your place." Why? Because He is the one to be served, and we are the ones to serve. 

There is a hierarchy. This has been reversed. During the three years of public ministry, the disciples of Jesus tried to elevate themselves. They tried to be higher than the Lord. Their hearts were infinitely high. Deep in their hearts, they were alive. Jesus should have been alive there, but He was not. 

On this mental standard, we must establish a connection with Jesus and be able to declare that we have conquered heaven and earth, even if heaven and earth disappear forever, based on the foundation of eternal victory. But is there anything like that in the Bible? Rather, they betrayed Jesus, who came to this earth and lived for over 30 years. Thus, the environment became one where Satan again acted as the master. 

Although 2,000 years of history have passed since Jesus came and went, God has still not found the solution to exercise the authority of the universe before all creation and heaven and earth. If anyone thinks they have found it, please raise your hand. 

God's desire is to open the door of human hearts, settle in those hearts, transfer all heavenly feelings there, and plan everything concerning the earth through that heart. Yet, God has not yet met a person with such a heart.
Therefore, Jesus said that there is a kingdom of heaven in your heart. Before longing for the intangible kingdom, build the tangible kingdom! Before hoping for the intangible kingdom, complete the tangible kingdom, that is, the substantial kingdom! This is what Jesus wanted to assert.

Foxes have holes and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head, He said, which does not mean He had no home. It means He had no place for His heart. Jesus did not have a foundation where He could connect with others through His heart, rejoice with His heart, be comforted with His heart, or empathize with His heart. If there had been such a person, Jesus would not have been pitiful. Even if He had to die on the cross, He would not be pitiful. No, if there had been such a person, He could not have died.

Thus, through countless seekers living on this earth, God’s work was to develop the palace of the heart. God has been coming to find us until now. He has come to this earth, a world of death. The Father has come.

Who did Jesus come to find? He did not come to find those in power like Pilate. He did not come to find the proud and powerful priests and teachers of the law. He did not come to find those who thrust out their chests and lift their faces. He came with a heart like that of a sinner, even though He was without sin, with a heart that, even if He had food, would not eat, and even if He had clothes, would not wear, and even if He had a place to live, felt He could not live there, saying, "Forgive the sins of the nation. Open the gates of death for all humanity. Relieve the suffering of the nation." He came to find those who were crying out from that perspective, not those who punished, rebuked, and insulted the nation that had betrayed God.

Because of this contradiction, God and the world are opposed; the place where the world rejoices is the place where God grieves, and the place where God grieves is the place where the world rejoices. Looking at the history of the Jewish nation, we can see that when the Israelite people rejoiced with the world, God was grieving. Therefore, God has been searching and struggling to find us. He did not come to this earth with the authority of a prince. He came from the very lowest place on the earth.

You must understand the history of restoration well. What kind of age was the Old Testament era? It was an era where God worked through servants. It was an era where God worked through angels, that is, heavenly servants. What kind of age is the New Testament era? It is an era that has passed the age of servants and has risen one step higher than the Old Testament era. The New Testament era is when God, after 4,000 years of hard work, sent His Son to work in an environment prepared by the servants who had laid the foundation to protect the Son. This is a continuous ascent.

What kind of servants were they? They were faithful servants, those who were devoted to serving God during that time. This must be understood. Who was welcomed among the chosen Israelites of old prophets? After 4,000 years of hard work through the devoted servants, the Son was sent.

What did the Son do when He came to this earth? He did not seek glory. Therefore, it is unforgivable for many Christians today to hope for joy or satisfaction centered on themselves. Who did Jesus, the Son, go to find? Did He go to Pilate's court to argue with Pilate and discuss the great principles of the universe? He did not. Did He kneel with the high priests and discuss, "Hey! You are the one who has violated the integrity of Israel, chosen and established by heaven after 4,000 years of hard work"? He did not. Did He enter a village and gather the Israelite people, saying, "Let us live together forever"? He did not. Did He say, "The reason God has worked hard for 4,000 years to choose and establish you is for me, so serve and honor me"? He did not. He was not exalted as the only begotten Son of heaven or as the crown prince of heaven. Who would have thought that Jesus would fall so low? Who would have thought that all prestige and environmental factors would fall so low? Would God have looked at that and said, "Oh! Well done"? No, that is not the case.

Jesus, who came to this earth, knew that the servants had established loyalty according to the laws over 4,000 years, so He could not establish His own prestige before them. Even if He had to suffer and face a miserable environment, He could not abandon the connection that He was the Son of God and that God was His Father. And knowing the heart of God, who had been searching for the Son for 4,000 years, He could not help but say that He would be a filial son before heaven even if He had to die.

Thus, Jesus, thinking of the loyalty established by the servants, established the loyalty of the Son from the position of the Son. Therefore, even on the cross, He said, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will." (Matthew 26:39) He was determined that His body was not His own. God said, "I am the Alpha and the Omega," so the place He had to go was that place, and because He was made through Him, He had to live according to Him and walk the path to fulfill His purpose. Therefore, no matter what difficulties arose, He overcame all those difficulties to avoid leaving a historical sin of unfiliality before His original Father’s heart.

What is the Holy Spirit? The Holy Spirit is the Mother. And the Holy Spirit is a daughter before God. Thus, Jesus and the Holy Spirit appeared on this earth as the Son and Daughter of God. So what did Jesus and the Holy Spirit do? Your Son is Me, and Your Daughter is the Holy Spirit. Your will is to find the earth, to find Me, and to find the Holy Spirit, is it not? Therefore, Your will is with us, and our will is on this earth. We are responsible for this earth.

Because it was possible, from the day Jesus came, God’s work was transferred to Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Thus, if there is a nation that commits sin on this earth, Jesus and the Holy Spirit, as sons and daughters, have offered atonement to God on their behalf. We must understand that this is how they are coming forth.

We know that when the end comes, the Lord of the Second Advent will come. So what purpose will the coming Lord have when He comes to this earth? Since the age of servants has passed and the age of sons has passed, the Lord who is coming will come as the Father. He will come in the glory of the Father. What will He do when He comes in the glory of the Father? He will breathe the heart of the Father into each individual human being. It is not the heart of the Son. It is not the heart of Jesus. It is the heart of the Father.

When Jesus came to this earth as the bridegroom and received the bride, what did He have to do? He had to go before God and receive blessings. He had to embrace all humanity in the love of God and receive blessings before God. In that position, Jesus and the Holy Spirit could not go before God to receive blessings. To receive that blessing, they had to establish the historical standard of the Father on this earth. Therefore, the Lord of the Second Advent will come to initiate the work of the Father.

Humans must embody the nature and form of the Father. He will raise the work of the Father and breathe the heart of the Father into the hearts of fallen humanity, recreating the image of the Father. In Genesis 1:27, it says that God created man in His own image, in the image of God He created him; male and female He created them. It is not the image of Jesus. It is the image of the Father.

Where is the ultimate purpose of salvation? It is in establishing the image and nature of the Father. For that purpose, God has been working hard until now. You must understand the circumstances of God as He has gone through the path of restoration. Because of this, God has not ceased to come to find us, the pitiful humans living on this earth, who deserve to die a million times.

Today, you are not perfect individuals like Jesus. There are countless types of humans living on this earth. Religions are diverse. Therefore, you must understand that the form that the Father interacts with is also diverse. When reflecting on history, you must think about what kind of appearance the Father has come to find us. He has worked hard for 6,000 long years to find even one insignificant person. If I cannot fulfill the will of the Father who has come to find me and go to the spirit world, I must understand that God will have to face me again with a heart of sorrow.

Since humans started with an eternal heart connection, before God can have a moment where His heart and the heart of humanity meet and rejoice together, and before that can be applied to the value of the whole, God will always be sorrowful.

In this position, the Father is still coming to find humans on this earth. Even at this moment, while you are here worshiping, the Father is coming to find you. He is going to the places of death where the waves of death are crashing.

Why must God stand in such a position? Originally, humans and God were in the relationship of Father and sons and daughters. After creating the heavens and the earth, God poured all His utmost energy into creating humans. If there is a heart, He gave all of it; if there is a mind, He gave all of it; if there is a body, He gave all of it. That is why the Bible says, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your strength."

Why did God create Adam and Eve as such precious beings? Was it to make them do errands? No. He created angels for that purpose. Then what was it for? It was to make sons and daughters.

"I am the Father, and you are My sons and daughters. If you are sad, I am sad, and if you are happy, I am happy." He created us to be in such a relationship. Parents with children understand this. No matter how unfilial a child becomes and ends up in prison as a murderer, the parent's heart moves toward that child beyond the prison bars.

If fallen humans feel this way, how much more so for God, who exists as the original heart itself! No pain can remove this heart. No sorrow can remove this heart. No anguish or resentment can eliminate this heart. Because of this connection, God cannot abandon fallen humans and is coming to find us.

It turns out that He is such a Father. Have you fulfilled the mission of a son before such a Father? Have you fulfilled the mission of a daughter? We must reflect and lament that we were a wicked group who could not even think of such things. We cannot blame anyone. Even if there is a bitter enemy right in front of us, we cannot blame them. No matter how unjust our position may be, we cannot blame anyone. Why? Because if I could repay evil, then all humanity in this world would have to die. That is why we are told not to repay evil. Why? Because God cannot do that either...

Humans, who are in the position of children, have fundamentally committed wrongs against God, who is in the position of a parent. However, who can sever the original connection between God and humanity, which has become entangled emotionally? No one. Therefore, the work of salvation to save humanity is done with love, love. It is not faith, nor hope, but love. The last thing that remains is love. So if there are sons and daughters who can hold onto the Father, who has worked hard for 6,000 years, Satan cannot take them away. If there are sons and daughters who can say, "He is my Father," no matter how much Satan is an enemy, who can deny that they are the children of that parent? No one can.

Has God, who is in the position of a Father, ever played the role of a Father? He has not.

"My beloved Adam, my beloved Eve, you are my son and you are my daughter. Even if heaven and earth change, who can deny that I love you and you love me?" He longed for a position where He could say this, but humanity fell without reaching that time. That is why He wants to restore this. He wants to find it again.

God has come to hold onto the weeping nations with history. He has come to hold onto the nations that weep for heaven. He has come to hold onto the nations that are oppressed for heaven, and to those who are cursed and killed for heaven.

God knows the circumstances of humanity better than humanity knows itself. That is why He can forgive human sins. He knows the causes and effects of those sins so well that He forgives them and does not remember them. Moreover, He knows how the human heart felt when it sinned, so heaven cannot remember the sins.

The pitiful Father who comes to find His lost children. God comes out with this standard, starting from the very end. When fallen children were being oppressed, He became their leader. It was not Moses who stood before the Israelite people after being expelled from the palace; it was God who stood there. Moses was not the only one who cried. We must understand that God cried even more than Moses.

Sometimes I think that God is like a wandering minstrel carrying a heavy burden. This is indeed the case. He wanted to unload His burden on the Israelite people, but because they betrayed Him, He became a wanderer carrying that burden throughout the world.

Who could understand that aching heart and that boiling emotion? It does not matter whether a person is good or bad. Knowing or not knowing, having or not having knowledge is not the issue. Who will be the filial son or daughter who understands God's heart? Where is the family that will welcome God? Where is the nation that will welcome God? That is the issue.

The earth is vast, and there are many humans living on it, but there are no children who shed tears for the Father who has become a pitiful wanderer. To create such children, I must teach them that I am your Father and that I have worked hard like this and that. This is truly a regrettable fact.

Originally, God is the one who governs the entire universe and should appear before His children with infinite love. However, He has become a pitiful and sorrowful figure, struggling without ever having children. How pitiful is that! You must understand this.

As you saw today, when a very small orphan passes by in a pitiful state, if someone sees him and thinks, "There goes the Father," and sheds tears for him, that person is one who serves the Father. Also, when a beggar in ragged clothes passes by, if someone recognizes him as the Father coming to find him and thinks, "My Father is also passing by," and sheds tears, that person is also one who serves the Father. The principle that treating a passerby is treating the Father comes from there.

How can one become a true filial son or daughter? One must empathize with the circumstances of the Father. One must know all the circumstances that the Father has gone through in the past. Our Father is...
What kind of father is He? He is a father who sheds tears in front of the gallows when his beloved sons and daughters go to the execution ground. He is a father who weeps before the sinner, even though he is not a sinner himself. He is an exceedingly good father, and you must understand that He has never failed to participate in the places where the unfortunate people of this earth go.

The reason the father seeks out such places is due to the bond He has with humanity. When you pray from a comfortable place, you cannot receive grace. You must walk the actual path that can replace that father while recalling His image.

Do you know what Jesus prayed when He found Himself surrounded by His nation and betrayed? He did not pray, "Father, please bless me and let me live comfortably." Instead, every time He was cornered and chased, He prayed, "Father, it is so unjust. How many times have You walked this path in the history of humankind?" He prayed, "The tears I shed are the tears that represent You!"

A true shepherd, a true son or daughter, even if they are dressed in rags and wounded, will forget their own appearance and wounds and think of the father who has walked an even more miserable path, and they will weep with the father's heart. Only such a person can enter the Kingdom of Heaven. If you are a believer, you must be able to weep even when looking at a silent mountain peak. Why? Because when you look at that mountain and think of the time when God created heaven and earth, your heart cannot help but break. You must understand that there is not a single creature that God created that does not bear the traces of tears.

Every time you encounter a beautiful landscape, you should be able to call upon the father and shed tears. Why? Because the father has spent a long 6,000 years weeping for His sons and daughters. This is not mere imagination; it is a fact.

Even if your hand is a part of your own body, you cannot say you have experienced the father until you reach the level where you can forget that hand and weep while holding it. Do you understand what I mean? The left hand is the hand of a beloved son, and the right hand is the hand of a beloved father. Only those who are caught in the emotion of holding their own hand and crying out, "Father! My son!" will be able to enter the Kingdom.

When you pray, you must reach such a state. Have you ever entered that state? If you forget yourself and unknowingly weep for hours, you will come to know that heaven weeps as well. When you go beyond that state and call out "Father!" it becomes real.

There are many nouns for "father." There is my father, others' fathers, bad fathers, and good fathers. There are beloved fathers and fathers who are not loved. There may be fathers who seek to gain something from me. However, you must know that there is a father who weeps for you.

The father you must cherish and comfort in your heart is the one who has come through the brink of death, holding onto humanity. He has pushed through the decaying body in the world of death and has transferred His heart, His feelings, and all of Himself into our hearts, and then He wants to bless us.

You must absolutely welcome the father who has come through such a historical process. But where will you welcome Him? Have you prepared a place for Him? Where is that place? Where is the nation that was prepared to welcome God? Is the place where you live a place to welcome God? Is the country you live in? No. Why? Because there is no place on this earth that can be trusted. There is no place to find rest.

So first, I must center my heart and become an eternal and unchanging figure to deeply welcome the father into my heart. After welcoming the father into the center of my heart, I must establish a new family centered on that father, a society of the father, and become the father's home. Has this country become such? Has this world become such? Has any nation on this earth that claims to believe in heaven become such? No, it has not.

Then where will you welcome the father? It is deep within each of your hearts. If you have welcomed the father deeply into your heart, what must you do next? You must comfort Him. What kind of heart should you have to comfort Him? You must know that He is a father who has worked hard and has come to find you over 6,000 years. You must comfort Him knowing that He has come as a more tragic figure than any protagonist in a tragic film, and you must welcome that father.

Look at the father who has come from the family of Adam. The father wanted to establish Cain and Abel and conclude the great history of heaven's providence, but Cain killed Abel. How must God's heart have felt upon seeing Abel die? This is indeed God's heart. It was the same during Noah's time due to Ham's mistake, during Moses' time due to the disbelief of the Israelite nation, and during Jesus' time due to the disbelief of the Israelite nation.

I am a sinner who killed the father. Since the fall, humanity has woven a history of tragedy. God's providence is tragic. There is no comedy. Today, we are witnessing a continuous program of tragedy and the true horrors of tragedy. In the scenes of tragedy, who has fallen and who has wept? It is God. Countless prophets have fallen in place of God, and countless saints have fallen in place of God. Who is all this for? It is for me.

If we were to watch such a film, there would be no one who would not weep. Not only that, our ancestors killed Jesus, who came to this earth as the father of all humanity. We are the descendants of villains worse than murderers. Jesus came as the second Adam. Since the first Adam fell, He came as the completed Adam, the true father of humanity. Since the first Adam became a false father, the second Adam came as the true father to give birth to all humanity again. He must revive us. That is why we speak of resurrection and salvation.
