We killed Jesus, who came as such a figure, so we are murderers. We must think and pray about this. Oh! Father, I have nothing to feel guilty about is a statement we must abandon. You see, we are murderers who killed the father. We must understand this. No matter how stone-hearted a sinner may be, when they realize they have killed their father, they cannot help but weep at that moment. That is why salvation for all humanity can be achieved.

You see, we have not only killed the father but also the son, the servant, and all of God's people. We must feel this and repent. I have seen death row inmates many times while in prison. If they had a way to escape their suffering, they would do anything. If it meant saving themselves, they would kill a thousand or ten thousand people. Such a world exists. Every time I looked at that, I felt many things.

Historically, even though humanity has committed sins that deserve to go to hell, think of God's only begotten son, Jesus, who went to the gallows to save such people. Can we be forgiven for having labeled such a precious being as a rebel and killed Him? From a heartfelt perspective, we are sinners who cannot be forgiven.

We must stand in the position of realizing that among the sinners of the world, I am the greatest sinner. Only then can we understand even a little of God's heart and Jesus' heart. We are sinners. We did not welcome the father who has come. We pierced Him with a spear, placed a crown of thorns on His head, and nailed Him to the cross. It turned out that He was our father. Repenting of the sin of killing that father is the duty of Christianity. You must repent with such feelings and receive God's recognition.

When we look at the fact that Jesus came to this earth and was killed from a human perspective, how heartbreaking is it? We must help Him forget that heartbreak. The only thing that can help Him forget is the heart. Faith alone will not suffice. There is nothing but the heart.

For the sake of finding you, He did not mind the path of death; when the day comes that you are found, He can forget the pains of millions. He has come seeking you, and on the day you are found, He can forget the many hardships and injustices.

How deep must the father's heart be that He can say He will forget all that? Therefore, you must become a person who can be humbled and weep. You must become someone who thinks about how earnest His heart is that He would say He would forgive the fact of the unforgivable crime. Meeting such sons and daughters is the hope of heaven. Seeking such sons and daughters is the purpose of the providence of salvation until now.

We, who must now approach the father, must become people who do not know where to place our bodies while saying just one word, "Father!" Even in the world, people feel this way after committing sins, so how much more should we, who have a history of countless sins before heaven? Now you must hold onto that one heart and say, "Your sorrow is my sorrow, and Your joy is my joy. If You are sad, I will also be sad, and if You are happy, I will also be happy. If You move, I will also move, and if You are settled, I will also be settled." That is the only heart there is.

No matter how well you believe or how proficient you are in the Bible, it will not do. You must understand that earnest heart, that one heart. If such sons and daughters do not appear on this earth, God will not be able to stop His footsteps, which have been coming for 6,000 years, at any one place and unpack His bundle.

It does not matter whether the house is big or small. It does not matter if the place to sit is a rock. The connection of heart must begin from the heart, and the father comes to create that connection. Are there people prepared to welcome the father among the many believers on this earth? Think about it.

You have come here after being pushed and pushed again, struggling and struggling again. What is it that you must now understand? I do not wish for you to simply read the Bible a lot. I do not want you to pray a lot or do this or that. What I desire is for you to be someone who, if the father comes as a beggar, can unhesitatingly take on everything and bow down before Him.

You must become sons and daughters who can take on everything without hesitation, even if the father comes as a beggar. 

If you are such sons and daughters, when the Lord comes to this earth and ascends to the throne of the King of Kings with the glory of heaven, He will never say He does not know you. Therefore, you must become someone who can welcome Him in a pitiful position and possess the heart of heaven.

You see, the teacher always says that there is no difference between a wicked person and a good person. How much better can one be just because they are good? From God's perspective, it is worth less than a piece of paper. When you look at the 2.7 billion people from God's perspective, you will find that no one can complain. No matter how much they may be your enemy, you cannot complain.

After meeting the father who comes with such a heart, you must follow the path He walks and do the work He does. The father is longing for you to become such sons and daughters.

You have met God. Now that you have met Him, you must unpack the bundle. You are no longer prisoners. You must be sons and daughters who can take on the father's difficult tasks and say, "Father, where will You go? I will lead the way," and be eager to walk that path first.

God is longing for such sons and daughters. If such sons and daughters exist in this universe, God will pour out blessings wherever they are. If there is a group of such sons and daughters, He will bring all the grace that has been poured out upon all denominations in the world.

Thus, in the end, He will take away from those who have nothing and give to those who have. After that, He will judge the wicked ones in the historical process until now. Who will He set up to judge? He will set up His son to judge. He will establish conditions based on what His son has done and judge based on that standard. Therefore, there must appear sons and daughters who can welcome the father and whom the father can boast about before all humanity. Only then can He judge based on the sons and daughters.

It is not a judgment done haphazardly. He will judge by setting up sons and daughters who can face the glory of victory. Since we have struck the father who walks a miserable path, since we have betrayed the father, since we have said we do not know the father, He can justly do the same.

God judges after experiencing everything, so that judgment is a judgment of justice. Do you think God sits on the throne of infinite glory to judge? He is not such a God. God experiences everything directly. Therefore, He is the God who knows human circumstances better than anyone and understands human feelings better than anyone.

You must be able to comfort the father who comes to you regardless of your social status. If you do not have an environment where you can feel the joy of having the father in your heart, both emotionally and physically, you will have no way to escape judgment when the Lord comes to this earth. You must advance to such a standard.

Among you who have come here, what kind of place have you welcomed the Lord? Have you welcomed Him even in a beggar-like place? If there is a son or daughter who, even in such a place, says, "Oh, how humble it is that the father has appeared in such a place," and does not know where to place their body, cannot raise their face, and feels embarrassed to show their ugly appearance, then heaven will hold onto them and weep, saying, "My son! My daughter!"

Have you experienced that? The Unification Church is not a group that seeks grace in glorious or comfortable places. We have come out to fight against those who seek grace in such places.

We must go. Where must we go? We must go toward the place where fierce storms are raging. If we do not go, the father will have to come suffering, so we must take the initiative to pioneer that place. Even if it is a battlefield where death and fierce struggles are taking place, we must go there. Otherwise, the father will have to come, and we must go even if it means dying and being torn apart.

We must go toward that place. We will not welcome the father in a comfortable place. We must understand that He is a father who comes to a painful place and become sons and daughters who can welcome that father, taking on all of His burdens and fully taking responsibility for the path of His suffering. Even if the number is extremely small, there is no need for concern. God moves through such a group.
If God were to turn away, He would not be able to turn away. If there is a nation that is confident in that field in the world, that nation will dominate the world. Moreover, it will govern the heavens and have the authority to judge even the heavenly hosts. It is a glorious thing that the Father comes with such a gift of glory.

Until many sons and daughters appear on this earth who can call upon the Father transcending nations, borders, and the East and West, and can take responsibility for everything, this universe cannot become the heavenly kingdom. 

The world is moving toward that place. In the past, all ideologies of the East and West had no relation to this nation, but they are increasingly coming to the forefront as matters of this nation. You must have felt this well through the recent summit. Although they are nations that have no relation to us, when they tremble in their hearts, we tremble as well. In this way, the world is approaching me. If you look closely, this world has appeared as a sacrificial offering for judgment instead of me.

Therefore, now you must become those who can take responsibility for everything and step up. You must become the protagonists of heart, not the protagonists of authority. You must become the protagonists of heart who are more tearful than anyone and more compassionate than anyone. What humanity ultimately desires is not the way (道). While they desire the way, it is not the ultimate object. It is not any sovereignty. Above all, do humans not desire happiness the most?

Let us consider what would happen if all of humanity were to advocate a certain ideology, and the world entered into that ideological sphere. Would everyone truly be at ease and happy? They claim to fight for freedom and happiness, but are they truly fighting for happiness and freedom? We know well that they are not. A very small group may be free and happy, but from the perspective of true happiness and freedom, those are merely illusions.

The heart, the source of life, can enjoy with the heavens, and if God moves, I move, and if God is determined, I am also determined, and if I can have the feeling of looking and listening together with God, then those sons and daughters are the happiest. Such people are needed in this era. That is why we desire it.

Until now, we have struggled to serve the Father who has labored in suffering, but from now on, we must have the heart to become the most filial sons and daughters who serve the Father who comes in glory. We must be able to serve Him not only in difficult circumstances but also when the garden of happiness opens and the Father appears before all creation with the authority of the Creator. We must have the heart to be filial sons and daughters even in the world of original goodness and glory.

Being filial sons and daughters is not only necessary in this era. It must be so not only in times of suffering but also in times of joy. Even if it is the time of glory, if dancing brings joy to the Father, I must dance to comfort Him. If singing brings joy to the Father, I must sing to make Him happy. I must be able to do that. At least, I must have that kind of heart.

To lead the Father to a sad place, to make Him walk that path quickly, is why we are making Him walk that way. After passing through such a place, we must have the spirit of sons and daughters who can boast before the Father, saying, "This is my son, this is my daughter," before all creation. We must have that spirit, and after fulfilling the loyalty of filial sons and daughters before the Father who sits on the throne of glory, we must have the heart that all of creation can bow their heads.

If you have such a heart, who could look at you with disdain? If you do not try to serve the Father in a place of suffering and have that heart from the beginning, Satan will accuse you. However, after going through such a process, you can be proud. God recognizes that. But if you try to rise up leaving God behind, everything will fall apart.

We must serve the Father of suffering first before we can serve the Father of glory. Just because we have served the Father of suffering does not mean we have served the Father completely. We have not served Him at all. Even if I, a pitiful being, walk the path of sorrow in silence and call out to the Father with the heart of being His son, "Father!" that is merely a trigger for the Father to shed tears. Therefore, we must serve the Father not only in such places but also in the places of glory.

We must go to a place where we can fully qualify as sons and serve the Father in glory forever. God is also looking for sons and daughters who can participate from the place of suffering to the place of glory. Wouldn't that be the case?

From this perspective, there is no nation as pitiful as our Korean people in the world. But you must never lose heart. Even if we are in such an unfortunate and difficult situation, if God comes here, we can serve the Father from a place closer than anyone else.

If our hearts are thick, we must be able to comfort the Father who comes to this difficult environment through that heart. If that happens, when we go to heaven, we will become those who can serve the Father in the most glorious place.

So do not be discouraged. 

No matter how the world boils over or how society changes, our single-minded devotion toward the heart of God must not change. Even if my body is torn and falls apart, the promise to serve the Father must never change. Even in such places, when I meet the time of glory, I must have the boldness to say, "I will do this and that for the Father." When I go to that country, rather than saying I will receive glory and serve, I must be able to say, "I will do this." 

You must understand that even the smallest thought of considering the Father as a child can remove the grief of 6,000 years and become a proud hope. 

You must know that you should advance to a place where you can serve the Father who comes and elevate Him as the Father of glory, and go to a place where, instead of the Father, you can say to Satan, "Hey! You scoundrel!" and make Satan flee.

<Prayer> Father, please forgive us for the countless tears we have shed because of our difficulties. When we were in trouble, we gnashed our teeth and tore our hearts. Let us know how unacceptable our behavior has been before You, Father. Father, let us understand that such things are fitting for a traitor who forgets the sorrow of heaven, but are unthinkable for those who know the sorrow of heaven.

Even when we are sad, let us rejoice; even when we are in difficulty, let us rejoice; even if we die, let us be thankful, for that is the only way we can take responsibility before the Father and avoid shame before the image of the Father who comes.

Now, the question is what kind of position we are in. Have we welcomed the Father who came at any time, fed the hungry Father, given drink to the thirsty Father, clothed the naked Father, sought the Father in difficulty, and visited the sick Father? Such a place is always a place where we can serve the Father. It is a glorious thing. 

You said that what is done to the least of these is done to You. 

Father, we have realized that our own will cannot be fulfilled. Let us understand that the whole is needed beyond our individual selves. 

We have understood that we must become the sacrifice of the whole, and that sacrificing the small for the great is a historical principle. Moreover, we have come to know that to establish the will of heavenly providence, great sacrifices must be made, so let us suppress our own sorrow and worry more about the Father’s sorrow, suppress our own worries and worry more about the Father’s worries, suppress our own grievances and worry more about the Father’s grievances.

If we become such sons and daughters, we will come to know that the heart of heaven will be with us. 

We were those who abandoned You when we had our own pain, and we were those who cried out to You when we had our own sorrow, and we were those who appealed to You to take on our grievances when we had our own grievances. We have come to know that this is not the way of filial sons and loyal subjects. Even if we find ourselves in a sad place or a place of death, if You are suffering from grievances, we must become those who bear that grievance. We have come to know that even if we stand in a difficult place where it is hard to stand on this earth, if You are in such a place, we must make sure that You are not in that place.

Father, what more can I say? At this time, it would be good if even one person swears to become a son or daughter who represents You with their heart. If not, what use has there been in all our cries until now? Father! Open the hearts of these people so that You may come, and relieve the grievances You have accumulated on the path of restoration, and let the joy and glory of serving the Father with our hearts reach all of creation in this world.

We know that You have been looking forward to that day infinitely, so let us also be those who fight and cry for that day. 

Let us become those who can set the standard of heart to say, "I will serve the Father at the altar of glory." 

I earnestly ask and desire that we may be those who can run forward with that heart. 

At this time, I ask that all words be entrusted to You and that You personally oversee them, and that our lives be made Yours, and that You personally oversee them, and I earnestly ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<One with the Father> Ephesians 4:1-16 

<Prayer> Now we have gathered here with the heart of a child and with a longing heart like a hungry person yearning for food. We long for the embrace of the Father and for an hour where we can comfortably rest in the Father’s love.

We have heard many words until now. We have listened to the words of many people fervently shouting from the altar. We have also sought in various ways to relieve the burdens of our hearts. However, we have come to know that those things cannot be trusted with our lives, nor can they become a resting place where our entire lives can dwell forever. As times change, we have been easily swept away, and we remember that we have been like wandering children or orphans, searching for something new as the times change.

We do not ask for anything from the world. At this time, we do not want to boast of our own merits. We only long for a place where we can forget all of ourselves and call You Father, captured by the heart of being Your son, and we long for the embrace of the Father who says, "My son, my daughter." We look forward to the day when we can move the path of life that seeks such a place to the knees of the Father.

We, who have gathered here today, have lived many lives of faith, prayed many prayers, and received much training in faith, but we know that the more pressing issue is whether we have become living sacrifices. When we think of the amazing fact that the living Father’s life sweeps over our hearts and bodies and leads us forward in victory, we know that it must be embodied in our bodies to live, and it must be embodied in our hearts to achieve victory.

We are asking for this, and we earnestly hope and desire that You will grant it. 

Father, what can I say now? I have tried to say many things, but knowing that nothing of humanity can forge an eternal bond of life, I hesitated to speak. Father, please appear personally. May the heart of the Father that You wish to convey resonate with the heart of the one conveying and the heart of the one receiving. We have come seeking that place where we can be moved like the blood and flesh of the living Father, so please have compassion on us.

Now let the heart of the one conveying and the heart of the one receiving become one. We know that Satan works to exploit the gaps, so let us be those who can return to the heart of a child and, with a longing heart for the embrace of our parents, be allowed to rest in the Father’s arms.

As seen in the scriptures, let this time be one where we can long for the heart of Paul who cried out with anguish long ago, and for the appearance of the early church believers who followed him, and may we dash toward the world of the Father’s heart. I earnestly ask and desire this. I offer all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Word> The title I wish to think about with you is "The Father Who Wants to Become One." 

With the title "The Father Who Wants to Become One," I will speak briefly. 

The countless humans living on this earth all know well that they are insufficient to believe in themselves and boast of their own value to the world. In a position where they cannot believe in themselves, they are searching for something else they can believe in. 

We are those who, forgetting our own value, wander in search of something that can connect us to other places. 

If there is a person who can say, "I can believe in myself 100 percent and proudly boast of my value before the universe, and I know that this is the value You are looking for, God, please receive it," that person would undoubtedly be the greatest success in life. 

The heart and body in conflict 

Throughout history, many great figures and sages have come and gone, but no one has ever confidently proclaimed, "Believe in yourself and live like me," while believing in themselves and publicly declaring their own value. 

We wish to move toward a good purpose, a greater purpose. You will feel that even if we ignore the reality of our current living environment, our hearts strive to run toward that place. You also know well through the workings of your own conscience that the environment you are in cannot become an eternal resting place. This conscience urges us to go because this place we are in is not a joyful place, exposing ourselves as being inadequate for any purpose or value. 

We must deeply feel this reality in our lives. 

When the heart commands us to go toward a certain destination, if the body cannot follow, it becomes a loser in the battle between good and evil, and one who is cut off from the heavenly and human worlds. On the other hand, those who act according to this command and step over their environment are surely those who can contribute something in history and leave something before the God who governs the whole.

The heart that urges us to go does not change with time and does not change even if the environment changes. However, when someone asks, "Can you boast before the world that you are a prince of rest?" everyone will have no choice but to answer that they cannot. 

Then, was this the fate of humans created by the heavenly motive?
is not. Therefore, humanity has repeatedly traversed the history of struggle through ages and centuries in pursuit of a higher conscience. However, we are still moving toward the world of purpose without having resolved it. When you finish your day's work and return home to reflect on your daily routine, if you can smile contentedly in your heart and say, "Heaven, Earth, and all mankind, may you emulate this joyful heart of mine," can you do that? Originally, we hope our hearts would be in such a place, but since we are not there today, this is lamentation, misfortune, and resentment. The heart longs to resolve the issues of my life and the whole, yet I am dragging a body with no internal conditions resolved and trudging through the fate of life, which is a pitiful human condition. Because our bodies and hearts are in this position, every time we are urged and stimulated to move toward a great purpose, our bodies resist. If we do not clarify our position to confront whatever makes us resist and begin to resolve that issue, we can only conclude that all problems of life are impossible to resolve.

The Fallen Human and the Path of the Way
How did all this come to be? Humanity did not start from goodness but fell into evil in the process of moving toward a good purpose, and thus it must break away from that evil. This is the path we humans must take. We must clearly recognize that we are descendants born of fallen ancestors who have created such a path. No matter how accomplished a person may be, boasting of their glory in the world, they too are descendants of a fallen lineage and are undoubtedly a race that must fall. Because of this, there is nothing more shameful and no way to maintain dignity. However, when we deeply feel that we are such beings and mercilessly strike ourselves, from there, a new mental revolution begins to sprout. Heaven is searching for such a person.

If humans had originally been such beings, they would not appear to be indifferent to God, the Father, who wishes to become one with them. If they had originally been such beings, many lives would have shed blood throughout the historical process, clearly demonstrating that God is a good God who pursues the purpose of goodness. However, that is not the case.

We are in a state of lamentation, but we possess the motivation to aim for goodness. If there is an absolute being who created the great universe, that absolute being is urging us to move toward that place through our hearts and consciences without rest, whether we are awake or asleep, eating or resting. Therefore, what is conscientious is valuable. No matter how satisfying one's environment may be, the moment one feels something stirring in the heart and sadness creeping in, it is a moment when the original movement is urging us. To feel such things and to struggle and seek to resolve oneself is the path of religion.

Those who walk the path of religion are not the leaders of their time. They are not people who cling to the trends of any ideology. They are not the warriors standing at the forefront to revolutionize any ideology. Those people are undoubtedly the ones who fall behind the flow of the times and refuse to go in the direction the times are flowing. That is why, until now, religious people have been advised to separate themselves from society, politics, and the ideology of life. Those who make the decision to leave their social or living environment, and those who feel emotional conflicts and sorrows there and turn away from them are the ones walking the path of the Way.

So, what is a person of the Way? Even if they remain in a luxurious and splendid position, they are the ones who can weep in that position. What is the heart of one who knows the Way? No matter how powerful they may be and how they may be in a position to move the entire world, in their deep heart, they can shed tears unknown to others. Anyone who does not possess such a heart, regardless of any society or organization, cannot be called a true person of the Way or a true religious person.

If one is a believer in God and follows the Lord, even if they are in a position of glory, they should not take that position as the ultimate foundation of satisfaction and rest, but should be able to shed unknown tears after passing through that position. Only such a person can be said to walk the path of the Way. However, because those who should walk such a path cannot, religion has been pushed aside and chased away. Why is this so? It is because humanity, destined to leave the place of sin and return to the original place, is in a fate that cannot go straight but must turn back instead. So why has humanity come to be in such a fate? It is because of the fall. The world has become one that has fallen and rolled down, so it must seek to rise again.

A nation that knows how to respect history can maintain its national character. A nation united on the basis of historical sentiment cannot be subdued by anything other than a leader who possesses a sentiment greater than that. Even if there are sages and loyal subjects who have upheld history and integrity, they cannot be subdued by anyone who does not possess a sentiment greater than theirs. Therefore, when the times are evil, only after cutting off that evil can one be grafted onto any other standard. This is something we always see in the process of social development.

What then should we do from now on? We must go beyond the standards of loyal subjects throughout history and the standards of filial piety and virtuous women. Moreover, there is a purpose to pursue even after surpassing those. Although it presents an environment detached from the present world, it is meant to hand us over to the future world. This is God's program. It is to create the most loyal of loyal subjects and the most filial of filial sons. Even if they are rejected and excluded on this earth, it has been said that a time will come when they can be the ones who govern and enjoy the world of the heavenly kingdom that the Lord will establish on this earth.

In the world, there are people who are loyal for the sake of family, for the sake of society, and for the sake of the nation. Those who are loyal for the sake of the nation can establish a condition of tradition in leaving the national ideology to future generations. However, everything on this earth and in this world must eventually stand before the judgment seat. To surpass this, we are taught in religion to become loyal subjects and filial sons before God, who is the King of kings, the Lord of lords, and the Father of all beings, rather than just loyal subjects for a single nation or filial sons for a single parent. This is the principle of religion.

So why did God tell believers to abandon this world? Because this world is destined to pass away. Since God possesses an eternal heart, even if He is rejected in this age, there will be a group that can be praised for their value as filial sons and loyal subjects in the future, which corresponds to the sheep among the goats in Christianity. Therefore, we must transcend the standards of the world. Those who are determined to be loyal to that ideology and are eager to run toward that ideology are the ones who believe in the Way. Therefore, those who follow the Way must become the vanguard in running toward such a world. If not, they will perish. They will perish. No matter what the circumstances are, they will perish. Today, the world is in such a fate.

You have started as individuals, but you must hold onto the whole world so that the individual and the world can connect and become a world that can be both the beginning and the end. In other words, regarding what your original conscience wishes to achieve, you must reach a position where this world can indeed say, "Ah, so it is."

Power moves toward a purpose. Even in the natural world, there is no being that moves without purpose. Even the smallest chemical reactions occur for a purpose. However, can the power of conscience, which no one can invade, move without purpose? No, it cannot. Conscience must have a purpose.

The glorious environment where my heart can rejoice, rest, and dance with the protagonist of conscience is the heaven that humanity seeks. Heaven is not a separate place. Those who cannot do so will run away even if they are placed in heaven. That is how it is.

God has been holding onto the fallen humanity for six thousand long years. If it were up to people, they would have killed them millions of times by now. Not only would they kill, but they would douse them with gasoline and burn them without a trace. However, God has come to seek such humanity. What is the purpose of His coming? It is to unite with sinful humanity. From the position of the utmost goodness, He wishes to become one with the utmost evil in heart, mind, body, environment, and ideology. That is God's situation. You must understand what God's situation is. Think about it. If God were one who just punishes and judges for wrongdoing, there would be no need for Him. Such a God should not exist.

Therefore, you must start resolving from here. What kind of God do I believe in? He is not merely a God who judges sin but a God who possesses a sincere heart before judgment. If God were to judge from a position that lacks such sincerity, it would be a protest. If He were a God who only judges sin, one could protest. However, one cannot protest. Why? Because God judges with a heart that exceeds human sin a million times over, so even if humans are judged, they cannot protest. God is not the kind of being you know conceptually.

When it is time to newly recognize God
Until now, we have sought God, but we have sought the God of rituals. We have sought the God of the Word. We have sought the God of relationships. However, we did not know the God of motivation. We understood the God of relationships that appeared after the fall through the Bible. We knew how God treated our ancestors and how He treated the fallen descendants. However, we did not know God's situation of being unable to prevent the fall. We did not know the motivation that forced God to cast out the fallen Adam and Eve. Without knowing the motivation, we cannot resolve anything. The same goes for worldly matters. When there is a problem, we must understand the motivation behind it to resolve it without future regret.

Even if we are proficient in all 66 books of the Bible, if we do not know the God of motivation hidden within the scriptures, the God of process, and the God of results, it is of no use. The God of process can be known because He appears in the historical process. For four thousand years, how much effort did He put into leading the Israelite people out to establish the foundation for the Messiah? That can be imagined. However, even if we say we know the God of process, we do not know Him clearly. Without knowing the motivation, we cannot claim to know Him clearly.

Then what about the God of results? How will He judge? Can you rejoice without knowing what God's heart is like? No, it cannot be done. There cannot be results without motivation. Everything goes through motivation and process to yield results. This is the phenomenon of natural science. Humans did not create it. The principles of heaven are such, and God's laws are established that way. There is no such thing as mutation. There is none. It is orderly. The world of creation ideology is one where a substantial purpose is formed through a principled process centered on motivation. Do successful people succeed without a firm resolve in their hearts? It is necessary to pioneer the environment centered on the motivation of the heart and to push through unchangingly to reach the destination. If this is true for an individual’s success, how much more so for God, who created the universe?

Have you sought the creative God, not just the historical God? Have you known the God who had the motivation for creation, the God who governs the world that must be judged, and the God who must live with all humanity in glory and joy after judgment? You have not known. Even in the success of a single person, one must not separate the past, present, and future. The past must align with the principles of heaven and its source; only then can it be established as a historical tradition, and that person's actions can be boasted about alongside history into the future. When one deviates from that motivation, they will be judged at some point. Therefore, what we must understand today is the God of motivation.

So how should we come to know the God of motivation? How has God approached us, who are stuck in the fallen position? God has approached us, who are fallen in the historical process, with the heart of motivation and the heart of the future. While humans living on the earth did not know God, God did not forsake humanity. Even until now, six thousand years later, humans have not known God, but from the time of creation, God has treated humans as His sons and daughters. Because He established the principles of heaven with such a heart, He cannot break this created world. The providence of salvation is to restore what has been broken. It is necessary to patch up what has been pierced and broken. To patch it up, one must establish a connection as the completion of the intended purpose through the motivation and process. Until then, one cannot present themselves as a completed product before the universe and all creation. This is only logical, isn't it?

We must re-recognize. We must reawaken. Especially, the youth must make a firm resolution. In the historical process, we must fight and achieve victory. Have you felt that you are being used for something while walking the path of religion? Those who cry out here have felt it deeply. Am I being used by God today? Am I being used by humans? Am I being used by denominations? Am I being used by history? Am I being used by any established theological system? Which is it? This must be clarified. I have not seen any literature that clarifies this. I have not met any scholars who cry out to clarify this.

This nation is a pitiful and miserable nation that has no conditions of hope to present to the world. What I desire is that at this time when the world is asleep in ignorance, our nation must awaken anew. We must reevaluate history, reevaluate the times, and reevaluate faith to seek God.

Those who are used by people or any institutions or denominations may perish, but those who are used by God will not perish. Do you understand what I mean? If you are used for any desire in the human world, you may perish, but even if you are rejected by the world and excluded from the earth, if you are used by heaven, you may seem to perish, but you will not. Young people with purpose must think clearly about which path to take. Therefore, at some point, you must also critique your father, mother, and siblings. Because they are the fruits of your lineage. Do you understand what I mean?

God, who has become disadvantaged due to human fall
It is simple to know God who has moved since Jesus. Jesus is...
I have come through the heart of God for a thousand years. You all need to understand that. When God sent Jesus, He came along with Him. Even though Jesus may have left, God, who was with Jesus on the cross, could not abandon humanity, even though humanity crucified Jesus. Have you thought about the God who holds on to humanity and its descendants? If you do not possess something that can explain this, do not even dream of becoming a bride. 

We have come to know the Jesus of the Word. This does not mean you should unconditionally believe everything that is said by people here. It means that if something resonates with reason, is revolutionary in your heart, and has the potential to break down your current self and build something new, then you should hold onto that and believe it. Those who believe in Jesus must go through such a level.

You all are indebted people. God has made infinite efforts to hold onto fallen humanity. He has made efforts that you cannot even imagine. To repay that, even if you were to offer 2.7 billion people as a sacrifice at once, you could not repay it. You must understand that God, who has labored with a heart pierced by nails, has dealt with ignorant humanity with motivation, process, and purpose. His guidance is not like a traffic cop at an intersection saying, "Go this way, go that way." 

There are words in the Bible that God commanded regarding the righteous, and He gave those commands after going through thousands of processes. There were times when I could not bear to look at the Bible because I knew such things. Tears blurred my vision. When God commands humanity to do something, He does not do so from a comfortable position. God speaks those words because He has passed through that place hundreds of times. It is not a matter of saying, "Try it once." It is a matter of saying, "Try it hundreds or thousands of times." Only after establishing a standard that if you win in the fight against Satan, you will be guaranteed certain things, does God tell humanity what to do. That is the kind of God He is.

The command to die in the Bible was given only after God experienced the anguish of death. He can say such things because He has become the protagonist who can do so. If He were in a different position, a God who sits on a throne and commands while everyone suffers would be accused by Satan. The reason Satan cannot accuse is that God's emotional pain is stronger than everything in the world of Satan. Because He possesses eternal principles and eternal emotions, Satan cannot accuse. Principles cannot be broken. They are inviolable. God has carried fallen humanity with principled emotions up to this day. Do you understand?

Who is God? And who is the fallen race? That God is the Father of the fallen race. He is called the Father of all creation. This Father is a Father with sorrow. God has become a Father who follows behind a son who is dragged into prison for committing sins. Although He is known as a free God, His heart is filled with shackles that He cannot remove. You must understand that God has come forth with a heart that has worried about the death and suffering of His son for many years as if it were just a day.

It is resentful. Why have You become the Father of fallen ancestors? You are pitiful. You must pray like this. If there are sons and daughters whose hearts are overflowing with filial piety and appeal like this, God will hold them and weep. God does not want to meet us in joy. He is searching for sons and daughters who will hold onto their Father, who is torn and broken, and say, "Father, how much You have suffered! I resent that You have become my Father." That is the kind of God He is.

Even though everyone goes their own way and the times flow, the unwavering heart with which God the Father treats His children cannot be violated by anyone. The more complicated the situation and environment, the more God worries. Six thousand years ago, He mourned over our ancestors as individuals, but now, in this time when all humanity struggles in the pit of death, He is the God who has the most pitiful heart and mourns. Therefore, you are sinners who cannot help it. You are the ones who are severely unfilial.

The heart of God who is carrying out the providence of salvation. If you oppose the king of a nation, you are called a traitor, and if you oppose your parents, you are called an unfilial child. But how many times have we been traitors to the Lord of all lords and the Father of the universe? How many times have we been unfilial? Each of you should think about this. Therefore, the more you walk the path of virtue, the more you must strip off your clothes, and if that is not enough, you must tear your body with a sword and offer your neck to the gallows. This is the heart that a son indebted to God should have.

Jesus was like that. He did not say to follow others. When Jesus appeared before all people, He was dignified, but when He was alone, He shed deep historical tears. He is the protagonist who shed sad tears. Even while shedding tears, He was a prince. Such content does not appear in the Bible. Who knew His heart? No one knew. What I want from the members of the Unification Church today is to know the God of the original motive, not the Jesus that appears in the Bible, nor the God referred to as the Trinity. Only then can you know Jesus.

Jesus avoided the place of joy by Himself. He left His home by Himself. It was not because He liked doing so. It was because He was in an environment where He could not cry for His Father, even if He wanted to, and where He could not acknowledge His Father. Do you think Jesus went to a lonely place in the mountains because He disliked the Israelite people? No. Jesus was filled with the desire to embrace the Israelite people and express God's heart while wanting to weep together. However, there was no one who understood Him.

If you have received the bloodline of your ancestors, then even to this one cell, there is a burden of sin attached. No matter how you may think of yourself today, it does not change that. The more you go on, the more you cannot help but shed tears; you are historical sinners who cannot lift your faces before the Father.

God has come to us with a heart. He has come with a heart that says, "I am your Father, and you are surely my son." Then He came with a situation. He came with the situation that He must seek out sinners. Then He came with hope. This is what is called faith, hope, and love. 

In the Bible, there are nine fruits of the Spirit: love, joy, peace, patience, kindness, goodness, faithfulness, gentleness, and self-control. What is the essence of these nine fruits? It is love, patience, and faithfulness.

If you look into God's providence, you will see that He has come to seek humanity with a purpose. What purpose? To save sinners and create sons, giving them heaven and earth. He comes with such hope. After creating Adam and Eve, God blessed them to rule over all things. But did they rule? They could not because of the fall. Therefore, God intends to restore humanity to that position. He has come with such hope and such a situation.

God is not the kind of God who simply says, "Hey, you, why did you sin?" He is a God who knows the circumstances behind the sin. He is a God who wants to understand humanity's situation without considering His own. He has come with the sorrow of the sorrowful, with the pain of the suffering, and with the grievances of those who feel wronged. How much have you seen God through your circumstances? God has come into our living environment like that. Moreover, He has come with a heart. Even if you betray Me, I am your Father; that is the heart with which He has come for six thousand long years.

Then what is God's ultimate purpose? It is for you to be one with Me and for Me to be one with you. Jesus also said, "On that day you will know that I am in the Father, and you are in Me, and I am in you." (John 14:20) The purpose is to become one. How do we become one? We become one in heart, in situation, and in hope. For this reason, God comes to us.

However, on this earth, there are currently close to three billion people living, and not a single person knows God's situation. Do you know what God's will is? Do you know what God's desire is? Is it to believe and go to heaven? That is an utterly absurd thought. The one who shouts here does not believe in such a God. Do you believe in a God who sends a body rotten with sin to heaven? If so, then He is a contradictory God. Does He forgive sinners and send them to heaven? Where is the principle of heaven in that? No one has gone to heaven until now. They have only been able to go to paradise.

God's thought is to live happily with those who are one and to move heaven and earth together with those who are one for eternity. Therefore, God is seeking those who are one. No matter how well you preach or what you do, if you are not one with God, it is all fake, fake. There are many times when those who act according to the truth appear worse than the fakes. Look at the actors. They are all fakes, but they perform better than the truth. The problem lies here.

The Bible is not necessary. My situation must become one with His situation, my heart must also be directed toward where His heart is directed, and I must be able to embrace the heart that He holds. God is seeking such people. He is seeking those who are one. For this reason, the battles in history are not battles between humans to become one, but battles for God and humanity to become one. Throughout the course of history, countless tragic bloodbaths have unfolded, but you must clearly understand that they are not battles for humans to seek God, but battles for God to seek humanity.

When God appears as the judge of righteousness in the future, what will He do? He will say, "I have poured out My heart for you, but how much have you poured out your heart for Me? I have understood your situation completely, but how much have you understood My situation? I have done everything for you; how much have you thought about My will?" This will be the way to resolve the issue. It is not a matter of saying that if you eat a piece of fish that is forbidden in the Bible, you will go to hell. The world of heart transcends laws.

When we stand before the judgment seat of righteousness, Satan will accuse us. Go to a court once. There is a judge, a prosecutor, a defense attorney, and charges. The judgment seat of righteousness is similar. Satan, like a prosecutor, accuses you. Jesus is your defense attorney. No matter what you did in the past, He is sweating to defend you. However, because humanity has brought forth six thousand years of sinful history, there is no way to defend it. There is no way to be on the side of righteousness. The burden of sin is too great. It is only conditions that can be caught by Satan. What will happen then? The Father is longing for a person to come forth to settle this. The Lord is praying about this in the other world. He is not worried about a few people falling in this world. He is concerned about establishing the great way of heaven's principles. Does God perish because one person goes to hell? No. Salvation is personal, but the great way of heaven's principles belongs to all humanity, so even if one person must be sacrificed, the great way must be established. That is why Jesus is praying.

When you read the Bible or pray, do this: Understand what God's will is, what God's situation is, and what God's heart is. Hold onto the one that God has mourned over the most throughout His life. Then you will go to heaven. Everything else is unnecessary. What is God's greatest grievance? What is His greatest sorrow? What is His greatest joy? The Bible shows no joyful events. It is filled with sorrow. Has there been a time of joy since He has been rejected and driven away? What was the saddest thing in the work of the Father? The problem lies there. If you resolve that, you will be fine. A true friend is one who understands the sorrow of the other through the heart. A filial child cannot be someone who can be filial in a position where anyone can be filial. The same goes for loyalty. You must understand this. You must understand what the essence of God’s six-thousand-year journey has been.

God has approached humanity with heart, situation, and hope. God knew our hearts one hundred percent, understood our situations one hundred percent, and knew our hopes one hundred percent, but He could not speak. This is God's situation. Why could He not speak? Because if He did, Satan would understand first. 

If a rich man has an immature child who knows nothing, would he tell him, "There is treasure here, and there is treasure there," while allowing a servant who has betrayed him or his enemies to inherit it? Would he let them have it? That is the position of Satan. If God tells everything, Satan will know it before God's sons and daughters can act.

Why is that? God is separated from the fallen world. Who rules this earth? Satan rules it. The prince of the air, Satan, rules down to the earth. Therefore, there are many enemies on this earth. If the enemies know what God has commanded His sons and daughters to do before they can do it and do it first, then when they demand it, it must be acknowledged because of the law of righteousness. 

That is why the Bible is written in parables. It is written in parables. It is unfair and frustrating. When you hold onto the difficult questions of the Bible and pray, "Father, why has it come to this?" the person speaking here has felt that. When you appeal, "Father, how have You become the Father who must save all humanity?" God will say, "I have a situation that is more pressing than yours."

When you come to understand this, you will realize how shameless it is to think that just believing will get you to heaven. Have you ever had the Father who wants to be one with you? Have you ever fought to become one with the Father? Not even once. Even if you say you have never done so, you cannot refute it. However, how much has heaven labored to become one with us? You must understand this.

Look. God has urged the Israelite people to become one with His will. Then He gave the hope that you, the Israelite people, who have been prepared for four thousand years, will rule the world. He blessed Abraham, saying that his descendants would be as numerous as the stars in heaven and the grains of sand on the seashore, filling the earth. He came with hope. Then, in the time of Jesus, He came with a situation. In the Old Testament, He gave the hope that the Israelite people, who had no nation, would become the center of the world, a kingdom of priests. He gave hope to those who were going forward.
God has come again with a situation. Who brought the situation? Jesus brought it. He has come to defend your situation. Once the defense of the situation is over, what does He do? He unites hearts. This is why the Lord of the Second Advent comes. The standard for that is love. In the end, it is love.

So, what position do we find ourselves in? Are we in a position to know the heart, the situation, and the hope? We are in a position of ignorance. We are foolish and ignorant. We know nothing. This is the God who suffers for those who know nothing. Until now, we did not know this God. However, God has a heart and leads the entire history from one to the world, striving to create a time when He can love the whole as a Father.

In the Old Testament, He sent servants to instill hope, and in the New Testament, He sent His Son to communicate the situation. The Lord who will come again will come with the heart of the Father. It has been said that He will come in the glory of the Father. When He comes in the glory of the Father and establishes the standard of the heart, that will be the end. After establishing the conditions of the heart both on earth and in heaven, it must be proclaimed before the universe. You must declare, "You are my eternal and unchanging sons and daughters." This is the feast of the Lamb.

Dear friends, how should we face the end? Christianity teaches us to hold onto hope and to endure. It tells us to endure for fear of breaking the great path of heaven if we cannot bear it. Look at Jesus, Stephen, or the twelve apostles. They were torn apart and suffered all sorts of things, but they endured. They endured while looking forward to a day of hope. Those people were our ancestors. Hold onto hope and endure. Bet your tomorrow and endure. To know the situation, be fully devoted. The Lord died for you, so be devoted to the end.

God, who is striving to love a chaotic world, says to love, to be devoted, and to be earnest. This is to connect God's heart, situation, and hope. However, the time of hope has not yet come for us. The Lord of my heart has not come. There is no one to understand my situation. Thus, when the global time comes, they will work for unity. From Abraham to Jacob's family, Moses' nation, Jesus' world, and the entire universe, God is working to create one. You must understand that history is flowing toward one world to create this created world.

From this historical perspective, today is being unanimously called the end. If we make a mistake, we are in immediate danger of annihilation. But there is heaven. The judgment is the clash between good and evil, the two highest opposites. That is a historical battle. Look, when we examine history, after Adam and Eve fell, God established Cain and Abel to restore the fallen family of Adam and Eve.

How does restoration happen? God says to love those whom He loves. It is about the heart through love, the situation through love, and the ideal through love. In other words, it is love through the heart, the situation through the heart, and the ideal through the heart. With such a heart, God sought Cain and Abel instead of Adam and Eve. 

Cain was to love Abel. It was about grafting. This is where the game of grafting began. It should have concluded in unity here, but Cain killed Abel with a stone. The history of war began here.

Therefore, until now, history has been one where good people are killed by evil people. Evil strikes first against good. Generally, when two people claim to be better than each other, the one who claims first is the bad person. This is true 80% of the time. Good does not strike first against evil. In Korean history, treacherous officials attacked loyal subjects, not the other way around.

Where did this struggle begin? It began in the family of Adam. If Cain wanted to receive God's love, he had to be grafted onto Abel, whom God loves. It means absolute obedience. Only then can he subdue Satan, who betrayed God. Although humanity was blessed to govern the universe, because humanity fell and two relationships with different bloodlines emerged, the world unfolds in two directions according to this principle.

Thus, God established Abraham as an individual whom He could love. It would have been better if Abel had been established, but because Abel died, God found one person who could be a perfect entity to be loved, as the ancestor of faith who could replace heart, situation, and hope, and that was Abraham. God's providence is that all humanity must submit to Abraham, whom God loves. If you submit before the person whom God loves, you will be saved; otherwise, you will go to hell. Therefore, God established Abraham and said to become one with Abraham's family. If you do not become one, you are an enemy. It was said that if Abraham received circumcision, he would become a son of God; those who do not receive it are all enemies.

In Moses' time, there must be absolute obedience to Moses' words. Whether they are good or bad, everyone must be grafted onto Moses. To be grafted, hearts must be the same, situations must be the same, and essential hopes must be the same. If Moses said to die, they should have the heart to die; if he said to live, they should have the heart to live; if he said to do something, they should have the heart to do it. If they had extended such hearts through the situation to the foundation of hope, they would not have perished. But what happened to the Israelite nation that rebelled against Moses?

After 4,000 years of labor, Jesus came to the chosen Israelite nation. Jesus came to graft the nation and people before God with His heart. He had already grafted the Israelite nation to a hopeful standard, and He was trying to graft them deeply into God's heart through the situation. However, they could not communicate the situation and left.

Humans have fallen and received different blood, so they are like wild olive trees. Therefore, a single son must emerge who can respond like God's marrow, who can be angry, and who can say, "You are my flesh and blood." Then, all humanity must unconditionally submit before that son. To be grafted onto the true olive tree, the wild olive tree must be cut.

To become a perfect tree, there must be more than three. Among the three disciples centered on Jesus, which one was unworthy that He did not speak to them? No, He wanted to talk about the deep tragic heart of heaven at the right time, but He could not because they might not be able to bear it. He wanted to express God's life, God's love, and God's entire ideal through the three disciples, but they could not bear it.

As a result, the Israelite nation became a nation without sovereignty. This was due to the sin of killing Jesus. If the Israelite nation had received Jesus as the King of Kings and obeyed absolutely, the world would have already been conquered by God. Just as Moses' successor conquered the seven nations of Canaan and made them surrender, it would have been conquered without a problem. If that had happened, would the chosen Israelite nation, the future Christian believers in Jesus, have been slaughtered for 2,000 years? That would be utterly unjust. They must receive retribution for killing Jesus. It is said that the sins of ancestors go down to the third and fourth generations, so they must all receive retribution. This must be cleared within 4,000 years. Moses also came out after four generations in Egypt. Everything moves based on the principles of heaven and earth.

Having gone through such history until now, there is no one on this earth who has been grafted to God in heart, situation, and hope. Therefore, the Father cannot immediately treat us as sons. Why? Because we have fallen and been separated. Where does it say that God must fight according to the original ideal of creation? God did not establish such an ideal. Therefore, He sends servants to fight. Humanity has fallen to the position of servants, so He works to raise them to the position of sons who can communicate the situation by winning the battle there. The history of the Second Advent is to graft the heart.

The earnest heart that cries out, "Lord, come!" must pierce through heaven and earth. Only with such a heart can one be on the side of heaven. For that time, God has been working until now.

What is the end time? It is the time when heaven strikes this earth with all its might after 6,000 years of effort. It is a time when the utmost sincerity must be poured out. It is the time when the son and the servant unite. The son and the servant fight from the same position. Moreover, the Father joins them. The time when the Father, the Son, and the Servant all come out together is the end time. The Father has come out, the Son has come out, and the Servant has come out, so it is time to prepare the heavenly household. God originally created Adam and Eve as children and the archangel as a servant. Centered on the Father, the sons and daughters and the servants are moving toward a global completion time where they can unfold horizontally.

Thus, in the end time, there will be those who say, "I am Abraham." Go to a park like Pagoda Park and observe. What do they say there? They all speak with motives. "I am Paul. I am Jesus. I am God. I am something." Why do they say that? Because it is the end time when the servant, the son, and the Father can meet, a time for total settlement. The leaves, branches, and trunk must all be grafted together and come to life at once. The trunk is the Father, the branches are the Son, and the leaves are the Servant, all appearing at once. The trends of the world are heading in that direction. The history of God at the end is to raise those who have been grafted through the heart as the main characters of this world.

Today, the ones who will take charge of the world are neither communists nor democrats. They are those who survive by being grafted to God's heart, situation, and desire. This is the essence of the Bible. The ultimate destination of history must manifest in such a way.

Until today, the virtuous have been trampled. At one time, the upper class succeeded, and during the warlord era, the middle class succeeded. Now is the time of the workers and farmers. Even in companies, there are unions, and workers are asserting themselves. The time will come when the virtuous will rule. Only then will God be fair. God has been preparing for that time for a long time.

So what will God do? He will establish servants and sons and daughters, embracing them as a Father, shedding historical tears while reflecting on the past, and expressing His overflowing hope, painful situation, and sorrowful heart. In that moment of embracing the Son and the Daughter and establishing the Servant, we must long for the image of God who can look back on history and smile.

"O Satan, where is your power? O evildoers, where is your authority? Retreat before the righteous judge of justice." At the end, we must recognize the God who has labored for 6,000 years to become one. He is the God who asks to be recognized at least once in 6,000 years.

"You are my Father, and I am your son and daughter." We must be able to shed tears and express our gratitude for the Father who has labored so much for us. We must acknowledge that the efforts of our ancestors, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, were for us. We must go through the process of being unable to find a place for ourselves.

I do not have the heart to host the protagonist of the heart. That is what I long for. Since I do not know the situation of the one who has the situation, what should I do? "Do you like this? I have brought what you like." Have you tried doing this? "Father, I want to offer this. Father, please receive this." This heart must be earnest. "Is your will to save the Korean people? Is that your desire? Then even if I die, even if I cannot eat, I will save this nation and offer it before you." We must be able to say this.

To save not only all of humanity but also the millions of spirits in heaven, we must endure infinitely, hold onto the situation infinitely, and have infinitely sorrowful hearts. You must be those who can go toward this world with all your heart, soul, and body. When you realize that the Father has come to seek you, you must be filled with tears and a deep sense of guilt and gratitude to cross over the peak of judgment.

Christianity began with repentance, but it is the greatest sinner. We must repent for not knowing the situation, the will, and the heart. God is asking us to take the blows that He should take and to settle everything on our behalf. This is judgment.

Christians preparing their hearts, saints moving forward to resolve situations, and Christianity that must publicly declare the hope of one day. Now, we must give our hearts, our situations, and our will. You must clearly understand that by coming before the Father who has come to find us for unity, we can receive recognition as sons and daughters and cross over.
Please let us know that we are moving forward in this way. We have come to realize that we must become a group that can sing the joy of a thousand years after great weeping. We, who have suffered in silence, have felt wronged and have been scorned, before the Heaven that has prepared for such days, before that heart, before that situation, before that hope, we feel that we must die a million times, and even if we are torn a million times, we wish to be grateful and become sons and daughters who can appreciate this. We have come to know that this is the Father's wish.

When we cry out, we feel our strength is lacking. How can we express the heart of the Father? We earnestly wish to be those who feel the endless grievance of the Father at every moment, who look to the future and endure. If it is sad, Heaven knows that there is no one sadder than us on this earth. It knows that our lives are filled with grievances. It knows that we are lonely. However, because we know that this is the path you have left for us, we must be prepared to walk the path of tears, the path of iron bars, the path of death, and the path of adventure. Please allow many to have such conditions on this earth. This is your wish and my wish, so I earnestly ask you to allow us to create such sons and daughters even if we fall.

When we earnestly ask that the purpose of the providence you have left behind, our circumstances, and our hearts can be resolved as yours, we pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.

**15)**  
Jesus left everything behind  
John 16:25-33, 17:1-26  
<Prayer> Father, we miss your voice that used to command us. Please let that solemn voice that urged us to go toward the highest good move our hearts once again at this time.  
We miss your heartfelt circumstances that urged us to walk the path of persecution, the path of suffering, the path of tribulation, and to cross the hill of Golgotha to walk the historic path of misfortune.  
Father! We bow our heads before your gracious gift that calls us, who have grown up freely, lived freely, and become what we are, to resemble the most high Lord. Please have mercy on us.  
Even if we analyze our essence or character, there is nothing we can present before you, filled with sin as we are. We thank you at this time for gathering us and bestowing upon us your boundless blessings. We ask that we may experience and realize the painful circumstances and heart of the Father, who only requires a sincere heart and faith.  
Father, now that we have gathered, please look upon us with compassion. We do not wish to hear the words of any person. We have already heard many words and seen many people. We have seen many people and visited places of grace, but all have passed us by without forming a relationship with ourselves. Grace has passed as grace, and people have passed as people, leaving us as historical orphans alone. Therefore, we hope for a new spring to blow in. How much do you also long to grant such grace? Please let us be a group that gathers before the Father with a thirsty and impatient heart. We earnestly wish for this.  
What can we say? Before we speak, let us feel a deep emotion in our hearts that even we do not know, and let us be able to shed tears and cry out without realizing it. We know that such feelings do not arise unless Heaven moves, and we understand that one experience is more precious than ten thousand words.  
People today do not wish to listen to anyone's words. Having heard much and been deceived much, the saints of today and the people of the end times approach any words with a critical heart.  
We know that we cannot criticize even if we want to, and that the one thing that moves our hearts is the greatest authority and shield. You have moved us with this grace, made us repent, and made us submit. Are there your sons and daughters who are far away from you today, not able to be at your knees? Please let them be together. We know that even if it seems far from a human perspective, it is not even a sheet of paper's difference in your eyes.  
Is there anything that was not created by you? When you move with the authority of life, is there any existence that does not resurrect? Please let us, who are like a pile of skulls, become beings of resurrection and connect us even more through one heart. We have learned through your words that this is the greatest purpose of the heavenly principle. We have learned through your words that whether it is this way or that way, it is all one. We have come to know how much Jesus longed for a group that keeps the heavenly altar with the motive of one heart.  
Now, we have come before the Father in our insufficient forms, so please let us return with the heart of a child. How much can a human know, even if they learn? How much can they boast of what they have prepared? We know that we have nothing to present to the heavens.  
Father! Now is the time to share your words, so please be with us. Father, the words we read a moment ago are those that Jesus spoke when he felt that there was little time left on earth after living for over thirty years. He gathered his disciples and asked them to pray. Father! Although they are historically distant, please let us be a group that can face the image of Jesus at that time with a heartfelt longing.  
We know that what will remain after we die will be the reality of the heart rather than excuses or facts, so please manifest yourself to us, who must become the historical protagonists. We earnestly wish for this.  
We do not wish for many words, so please do according to your will, and let there be no gap between the hearts of those who receive the words and those who convey them. When Heaven moves, may our hearts move, and when Heaven is settled, may our hearts also be settled. We wish to be offered as a victorious reality that harmonizes and moves with Heaven.  
We entrust the remaining time to you, so please govern all things. We earnestly wish that the same blessing be bestowed upon our family members in the regions. We pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
<Words> The title of the message I would like to reflect on with you for a moment is "Jesus left everything behind." I would like to speak about Jesus, who left everything behind.  
We know that every being moving toward a single purpose, no matter how successful they may be on this earth, still has another hope remaining. Why is that? Because there is a protagonist who is the absolute being who established all fundamental truths of Heaven and earth and created Heaven and earth, and no sage or any other person can claim to have completed the standard by which even that protagonist can move. In other words, even someone who has achieved some success is still hoping for something new, and that is why I can say this.  
Throughout history, there has always been a need for leaders who can guide the people of each era. However, if God, who has the responsibility to send leaders to fulfill the providential goals of each era, does not send such leaders, then we cannot say that God loves humanity or governs humanity.  
Until today, there have not been many who could confidently say, "I have become this kind of person and achieved this kind of success" in the course of history. While no one has been without the desire to achieve fame in their lifetime, not many have accomplished what they thought and planned. Among those who have raised the banner of new revolution in the course of history, many have unknowingly fulfilled a century-long mission while being swept away by the environment and trends of their time.  
From this perspective, we can assert that even if someone begins to act with a firm self and conviction to achieve their goals, it does not happen as they wish. Therefore, we cannot deny that our fate and life path are not only carved out by ourselves but also flow along with some great current.  
We cannot deny that we are flowing through history from this standpoint, nor can we deny that we are struggling to find our resolution from this standpoint. We also cannot deny that the world is moving toward some destination and that it is moving toward a certain time. In other words, all beings are moving toward a certain time, place, and environment, and they are longing for something that can conclude the purpose of human history by managing this time and environment. This is something that anyone with common sense can understand.  
So what time is it now, and what kind of environment is society in? And who will dominate and lead this time and environment? What kind of time and environment is being created in this time when democracy and communism are in confrontation? What kind of leader are we trying to meet by creating this time and environment? These are serious issues that intellectuals in the modern intelligentsia must ponder.  
In any case, this is a historical course that must inevitably be traversed. Why? Because there is a protagonist who has established a purpose and is moving history, even if humans do not know it. If there were no such protagonist, history could not flow toward the hoped-for time and environment, nor toward the center of ideology.  
Until now, national sentiments have varied, historical backgrounds have differed, and even the forms of life have all been different. However, as history flows, humanity transcends these differences and eventually breaks down the rigid foundations they have held and is swept away by some trend that revolutionizes all organizations of the time. This has been the case in the external continuity of human history, but behind it lies the purpose of some absolute being. Therefore, humans are being led out by an absolute purpose without even realizing it. This is the position we find ourselves in.  
Today, humanity is moving toward such a time. We are also moving toward an environment of peace. After establishing this, we must find a protagonist who can lead humanity into an eternal world of heart. We must clearly understand that history is flowing toward this. In reality, history is flowing in this way. So why is this created world like this? Most of the great figures and leaders of this land thought they could take control of this world and lead it to a certain time, but they have only realized this within a limited class or nation, and they have not achieved their goals from a global perspective.  
If God exists, then this great purpose must be fulfilled. If the time to achieve the great purpose of the world does not come, then God does not exist. The time must move, and the environment must move, so that one person can govern all humanity centered on the heavenly principle. If that cannot happen, then the world created by God will remain in an incomplete state. There can be no such thing as the ideology of creation or anything else. Furthermore, all statements about humans being the lords of creation and the rulers of all things will become false. Therefore, in the end, there must come a time when such a person is established to handle history, manage the times, organize the environment, and restore character.  
From this perspective, we can immediately discern whether any religion or ideology can become global. In this light, Christianity occupies a unique position. You were born as a Korean. Some may consider being born as a Korean to be extremely unfortunate, but I do not think so. Why? Because as long as there is a God who seeks to establish a purpose, a time, and an environment, it is the same no matter where you are. Therefore, there is no need to lament being born in Korea. There is no need to lament that the situation in Korea does not match your heart and emotional life. There is no need to lament that there is no leader in Korea. In modern times, Christianity has also played a significant role in shaping the moral and ethical landscape of Korea. Today, Korea stands at a crossroads, where traditional values and modern beliefs coexist, creating a dynamic and complex cultural tapestry.

In conclusion, Korea's religious history is not just a reflection of its past but a vital component of its future.
