It influenced both ideology and sovereignty. Regardless of where the origin of religion lies or who its founder is, the country that has blossomed with religious culture is Korea. Buddhism originated in India but came to Korea through China, influencing the state and sovereignty and engaging in power struggles. Later, during the Joseon Dynasty, Confucianism came and dominated the sovereignty of the nation and organized the social system. In modern times, even though Christianity has only about 80 years of history in Korea, it is actively shaping this era.

When observing the flow of the world, it is essential that Eastern culture and Western culture converge around a single point. That is the purpose of heavenly providence. Therefore, in the East, Japanese imperialism emerged, and after about 80 years of history, including the Meiji 45th year, Taisho 15th year, and Showa 20th year, that imperialism collapsed. When Japan emerged as an imperialist nation, China and the Soviet Union (Tsarist Russia), feeling threatened, fought over Korea.

What was the motive behind the Sino-Japanese War? It was Japan's intention to use Korea as a foothold for continental invasion as it prospered in the Far East. The Sino-Japanese War was a conflict fought to satisfy their ambitions over Korea. It was also the Russo-Japanese War. Thus, Japan ultimately took control of Korea and ruled for 36 years.

Although imperialist nations like Japan, China, and Russia tried to swallow Korea and bring it under their control, they failed to do so. It seemed that Japan had taken Korea, but it eventually withdrew. Consequently, this nation welcomed a new day of liberation, and today it has become a stage where democracy and communism confront each other.

In this situation, the Korean people have come to understand what communism is and what democracy is. Communism cannot swallow the nation. They have seen the end of communism and know what democracy entails. They have seen it all.

From the perspective of the zeitgeist, what ideology can turn today’s Korea, this three-thousand-ri peninsula, into a stage of eternal welfare? Moreover, what religion can capture the hearts of this thirty million strong nation, not only in external matters but also in internal matters, where religious sentiment is strong? We must contemplate this. Today, we find ourselves in such a situation.

The Korean people have not seen Siddhartha Gautama, Confucius, or Jesus Christ, but they have witnessed the essence of the religions they advocated. They have not seen the founders of the world’s major religions, but they have seen the foundations of those paths. After seeing it all, we have come to realize that these cannot be welcomed by this nation but must be turned away.

Among them, Buddhism, Confucianism, and Christianity have taken shape and remain to this day, yet Buddhism fights as Buddhism, Confucianism as Confucianism, and Christianity as Christianity. So, what resolution will these paths ultimately reach to accompany the fate of this nation? This is something we must think anew.

From a historical perspective, Korea has become a showcase of world civilization. This Korea has encountered numerous ethnicities. The Essence of Faith
Our people have looked into the foundations of the doctrines established by Siddhartha Gautama, Confucius, and Jesus, but these did not fit this nation and have passed. What I want to shout before this nation is not to believe in Buddhism, Confucianism, or Christianity. Rather, it is to embrace Siddhartha Gautama, Confucius, and Jesus. On the other hand, evil is changeable. Whether it is democracy or any ideology, or any trend or religion, it should not change with the times. Unless there is change and development in the world of the heart, it must never change.

If not, I will appeal. I will even rebel against God. We Unification Church members must become such people.

I should not lament that I have nothing. Let us not lament that this nation has nothing. Look at history. Who would have known that Jesus, who traveled with fishermen who were marginalized and despised on the shores of the Sea of Galilee, would conquer Rome and become a personality that moves the civilization of the 20th century? Because history is organized around the heavenly heart, his teachings and ideals have remained until now, becoming Christianity, which truly moves the world.

Let us not lament that we have nothing or that we know nothing or that we appear to be poor beggars. Among our ancestors who followed the Way in the past, there were no well-dressed people. There were no well-fed people. There were no people who lived well in comfort. Even while being marginalized and chased, whenever they had time, they would bang their heads against the rocks and call out to God. They were people who could not live comfortably and would go into caves to hold onto God and cry out. Such people have governed the world.

So, what should the Korean people hold onto today? Not democracy, not communism, not established religions, and not any ideology. They must hold onto God. If God is alive in history and has the heart of the world, He must surely be seeking sons and daughters who have such a heart. If that is the case, the Korean people are in a position where they are most likely to be placed in such a position. Do you have parents? Do you have children? For those who came from the North, do you have land? Do you have a home? This is the situation we are in now.

At one time, I thought there was hope when refugees came and established churches. However, they too needed to have a heart that cries out and connects with Heaven, but instead, they became busy colluding with external ideologies and ended up like this.

If there is a God who is coming to this world today, He must surely be a God with knowledge, emotion, and will. Why? Because humans are like that. It is not a knowledge, emotion, and will centered on human ethics, but on heavenly ethics.

No doctrine of the Way has ever said to seek worldly success. It has said to suffer, sacrifice, and serve. It has said to be trampled upon. It must be trampled upon. This nation is the one closest to the standard of the Way that God is seeking. Therefore, we must negotiate with God. The time has come to negotiate.

Everyone talks about existentialism today, so diligently seek it out. Try to solve all the problems of reality. What happens? In the end, you will encounter despair and loneliness, and you will become nothing but an individualistic human. With the changes of history, you will change again. So, whether it is God or anything else, try to flow along with the currents of reality, and see what happens. It will not go as you claim.

Our nation has a potential national character centered on the Way because it has gone through thousands of years of history centered on various teachings. There is no nation with as strong a sense of faith as this nation. When placed in a lonely and pitiful situation, they immediately go to a fortune teller to ask. Even these days, it is the same. Regardless of social status, this nation has a strong sentiment that it must rely on something to live.

However, now such religions have been rejected by this nation. It is now time for a national religion to emerge. It is time for a national ideology to emerge. That ideology is not communism or democracy. It is heart, heart. This nation must now say, "God! Is your purpose not to find a completed personality both internally and externally? Is it not to establish the highest person who can communicate the heart of heaven among humanity?"

This nation is in a position far from worldly connections, so it is closest to Heaven. We must tighten our belts, wrap our heads, and pray. The Bible does not say to eat well and pray with a full belly. What does it say? It says that when you fast, anoint your head and go into your room to pray. That is good advice. This biblical word must be fulfilled. Even if other nations do not fulfill it, the Korean nation must. There is nothing left to do but that. From this perspective, something must emerge. Do you understand God's heart? If you do not understand your parents' hearts, you will be unfilial. If a son truly knows how much his parents love him and how much they have cherished him, he cannot be unfilial.

The Strategy of God

Even though this nation is in such a miserable and insignificant position today, it can deeply connect with God's heart, so we must pray. We must ask, "God, why has this nation become like this, and why has the world become like this?" There are many prayer topics. Did God come to this world to become a pitiful God? No, that is not it. Even those who seem to eat well, dress well, and stand in good positions in the world end up in terrible places when they die and go to the spirit world. Those who come here for the first time may not believe this, but those who were prominent in the world find themselves in terrible places in the spirit world.

Heaven is a world of heart. It is not a heaven of doctrine, nor a heaven of denominations, but a heaven of heart. Why does God want to find a people and believers on this earth? To create sons and daughters. What kind of sons and daughters? He drives out humans. 

He does this to create sons and daughters who can express, "My heart is like this." 

So, God's strategy has been like this until now. To take away a nation, God first matches the value of that nation. It is different from the strategies of the world. The strategy of a sage is that to find a value of ten, one must sacrifice ten. That is more beneficial. Why? Because if you sacrifice now and find it a thousand years later, the stage of goodness will be much broader globally, so finding it a thousand years later is more beneficial than finding it now. Do you understand what I mean?

God's work expands globally with the times. Therefore, if you sacrifice a good person a thousand years ago, you can find them back many times over a thousand years later. That is why good people are sacrificed. Jesus two thousand years ago was sacrificed for this reason. God sacrificed many good people to find many people at the end. Since many people have been sacrificed, and Satan has taken them, they can be taken back all at once.

So, what is the reason God wants to find them last? Even if they lived well and dressed well thousands of years ago, they can only be God's people. They can only be servants or subjects. The era when servants called upon humans to act is the Old Testament era. It was an era of servants. The prophets, that is.

Next, it is to elevate humans from being servants to the position of sons. That is why Jesus came as the only begotten son. If it is a matter of sacrificing ten servants of the servant era to find ten sons in the son era, then it is worth doing.

God is a cruel being. Because He looks at history from the perspective of a thousand or ten thousand years later, He does not mind many sacrifices. That is why Christianity has seen many of its believers sacrificed, regardless of the country they entered. God longed for sons and daughters who could stand before the final judgment with dignity.

If God's strategy is like that, then you must also be able to move in such a way to fulfill God's will. Jesus did so. He said, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will."

He was Jesus who understood that, so he prayed like that.

Now, even if we lose the Way, lose our nation, and lose our church, we must not lose God. Do you understand what I mean? It is okay to lose denominations. It is okay to lose sages, and eventually, it is okay to lose Jesus. What does Jesus save us for? To establish a bride and receive blessings before God. A bride is necessary to receive the blessings of God the Father. Without a bride, blessings cannot be received. That is the principle of heaven. Jesus also needed to find a bride to receive the blessing from God, saying, "You are my beloved son, you are my beloved daughter."

Let us serve the true Father of hearts.

Today, there are many who say, "I must become the bride of the Lord." In such times, we must resolve that even if we lose our denominations in the end, we must not betray God, only God. Today, in Korean society, the reputation of Jesus has fallen. The authority of Jesus has plummeted. However, that does not mean that God has fallen. Even if the name of Jesus has fallen, Jesus himself has not fallen. Now is the time when Jesus is being trampled upon. Then, there will be judgment. The good will pass through the lowly and then judge. Judgment is a time for a new beginning, so it must always be trampled upon.
It is good to come in and out of the church. However, what I want to say is that you should not just listen to any pastor's words superficially. You should not listen to the words of this young person speaking here with indifference. You should listen with your heart to something that you cannot deny. 

In the end, no matter what words you hear and swear by, they will pass away. Even if you swear by seeing someone and say, "Wow, that's good. I should do that too," that will also pass away. Ultimately, you must swear with your heart and spirit. Otherwise, you will not succeed. This is true even in the world. After seeing and hearing, saying someone preaches well or not is all fleeting. 

What matters is how our hearts are. Nowadays, when I see Christians, they sit there and criticize everything, saying, "Pastor A preaches like this, and Pastor B preaches like that." They have all become judges. Do you think they will receive grace like that? Grace is something that penetrates infinitely. Grace can flow endlessly. You must understand this. If you create discord, will there be grace in that? Whether the sermon is good or bad, when you enter that place, you must open the door of your heart. If you can awaken your original deep heart even from the passing breeze, that is grace. 

To all of you who are present here today, the person shouting here emphasizes that the time of worship is a more serious place than fighting with an enemy. Think about it. Can you attend a place where you seek to serve God without wearing your best attire? It is not just the outward appearance of attire; it is the attire of the heart. Even if your appearance seems pitiful, if from that heart, the heartfelt words and songs flow out, then heaven will work through you. When fallen humanity was expelled from the Garden of Eden, they were driven out with tears, but you must meet God with joyful tears and a smiling face. Those who have never shed tears of sorrow should not shed tears of joy. 

Therefore, you must not lose God. You must not lose the God you found with your own eyes. You must not lose the God you heard with your own ears, the God you felt through your own senses. Furthermore, you must not lose the God who seeps into your heart. This is something that no one can interfere with. No great person or authority can separate the God who enters through the heart. So, we seek that God who comes into our hearts. 

As I mentioned earlier, all beings are seeking something better. What could that be? It is not some great teacher. That teacher will pass away along with the world. Any current ideology or thought, whether communism or democracy, will also pass away. God is one, and He moves toward one ideology. The standard by which we must welcome God, who is coming to find His unified world, is not an academic standard, not an organizational standard, not a power standard, but a standard of the heart. 

The God whom millions face is more precious than one's own parents, more precious than the one they love, more precious than any business on this earth, more precious than anything that cannot be exchanged for this country or this world. 

Only those who have the heart to know that God will manifest in this world, and the world will become unified according to God's ideology and will. God moves based on that standard. Heart! The God who comes seeking the focal point of the heart is our true Father. He is our true Father. 

Let the Korean people hold the initiative in the world of the heart. 

Today, humanity knows the verbal father but does not know the substantial father. They say God is a God who grieves, but they do not experience it; they say God is a God who suffers, but they do not feel it. Therefore, they cannot be filial children. To know the heart of Jesus, who died on the cross, one must see the scene of Jesus on the cross and, transcending the boundaries of life and death, weep and say, "Lord, what is this?" Such a person is a disciple of the Lord. Those twelve disciples! Peter and the others! They are traitors. They are traitors. 

I once protested to Peter. What is this? What is so great about it? If Peter had faith and crossed the hill of death before Jesus died, that would be one thing. But God desires many sons and daughters on this earth who can do that. 

Now we must know that God is the God who divides, the God who is angry, the God who wields a rod, the God who weeps. When God grieves, we must also be able to grieve with Him. Such people can understand all that God is doing in relation to this earth. They know what ideologies will perish and what will happen. Don’t you know? Such people must emerge in this land today. 

Today, Christians and many seekers claim to have attained enlightenment. What does enlightenment mean? It means they are wandering, having not yet appeared in the human world, seeking the hidden heart of God that cannot be found in the emotional world of humanity. 

Faith, hope, and love will always be present, but the greatest of these is love. (1 Corinthians 13:13) However, true love has not yet emerged. 

When we consider everything, we are the ones closest to God, so we must first become those who are drawn to God in this age. We must be drawn. We must be drawn as heretics and monsters. Even if we become imprisoned for the sake of truth, those who can kneel and cry out, "Lord," in such a place will have the heavenly heart melt into them. The heavenly heart will melt. Does a prison cell block the heart of heaven? 

You may come here and sit without any feelings, but to reach this point of movement today, you must have gone through such a process. If you have not gone through it, you must be broken. If you gather people who are about to die and say, "This is God's heart, do you feel it? Do you understand?" then yes, there must be a way that can make that possible. Buddhism and Christianity can all go. 

It is easiest for the movement that can occupy God to emerge in Korea. So, everyone, if you are going to try it, you must become like foolish people. The person speaking here is the most foolish of all. I don’t know how you see it, but the world sees it as foolish. It is an utterly absurd fact. 

To find the standard of that heart, one must go anywhere. If in prison, they will go to prison; if in a cave, they will go to a cave; if in a slum, they will go to a slum. Even if there are century-old obstacles, if they can find God's heart there, they will have the determination to go there. This is the determination of the person shouting here. Can someone who enjoys life in a comfortable place and laughs truly hold God? Such a person cannot become a friend of God in a place where they bear the cross and stumble. 

In today's world, standing at the forefront of 20th-century civilization, humanity feels fear before the civilization created by humans in a place of shared destiny. In such times, what should we seek? It is okay to lose all doctrines and denominations. We must seek only God. What do we need to occupy God? It is not circumstances, material things, or any denomination, but the heart. We must occupy with the heart. Such a person may have nothing, yet they can move the universe and surely move God. 

If such people appear in the land of Korea, this Korea will be able to hold the initiative in the world of God's heart and command all humanity or even the heavenly world. I am confident that such a time will come. This Korea will become that. 

Nowadays, we see parents killing their children, children killing their parents, wives stabbing their beloved husbands to death, and elders killing people. In such an age, everyone says, "Go away, I have no concern for my parents." They say, "Go away," and those who have values greater than their parents or beloved children, those who can be grateful and shed tears even after losing everything in this world—such people, with such ideals, can resolve anything. Whether it is a fight or a financial issue worth hundreds of billions, nothing is unresolvable. 

We must clearly understand that God's providence regarding humanity is to act as a protagonist equipped with the authority of the Absolute and the heart of the Absolute. I sincerely hope that such a providence can manifest through the land of Korea before the world.

대하신다면, 그분은 절대자가 아닐 것입니다. 창조주가 되기 위해서는 그 창조의 목적이 있어야 하며, 그 목적은 창조주 자신이 지니고 있는 것입니다. 그러므로 하나님은 창조의 목적을 가지고 계신 분이십니다. 

하나님은 모든 존재의 목적과 가치를 세우시고, 그 목적을 이루기 위해 인간을 창조하셨습니다. 인간은 그 목적을 이루기 위해 존재하며, 그 목적은 단순히 개인의 생존을 넘어서 인류 전체의 생명과 관계를 맺고, 궁극적으로는 하나의 세계를 이루는 것입니다. 

그렇다면 인간이 이 목적을 이루기 위해서는 무엇을 해야 할까요? 우리는 이 목적의식을 가지고, 서로 연결되어 있는 존재들로서 함께 나아가야 합니다. 각자의 존재가치를 인식하고, 그 가치를 통해 서로를 존중하며, 하나의 목표를 향해 나아가야 합니다. 

이러한 과정에서 우리는 서로의 존재를 인정하고, 그 존재가치를 높이며, 함께 성장하는 길을 찾아야 합니다. 하나님이 원하시는 것은 바로 이러한 연합된 세계입니다. 

결국, 우리는 하나님과의 관계를 통해 이 목적의식을 강화하고, 그 목적을 이루기 위해 노력해야 합니다. 하나님이 주신 생명의 가치를 인식하고, 그 가치를 통해 서로를 존중하며, 하나의 세계를 이루어 나가는 것이 우리의 사명입니다. 

이러한 목적의식을 가지고 살아가는 것이야말로 진정한 삶의 의미이며, 우리가 나아가야 할 길입니다. 하나님이 바라시는 세계는 바로 이러한 세계입니다.

The unity of heaven, earth, God, and humanity through sentiment
People often say that there is heaven, earth, God, and humanity. The world is composed of this heaven, earth, God, and humanity, and they are each different. Heaven and earth, God and humanity are separated. Heaven and earth are distinct, as are God and humanity. So what should we do? We must reconcile.

We cannot live apart from the earth. Furthermore, we cannot live apart from conscience and higher heavenly principles. This is because conscience represents heaven, and the body represents earth. If there is an absolute being that possesses the value to harmonize heaven and earth, then humanity is established as the representative being that can form a heartfelt connection with that absolute being. Therefore, when the body that represents the earth, the heart that represents heaven, and the sentiment that represents God come together, all problems will be resolved.

I sometimes think this way. If we can unite the body and heart of humanity, and the purpose of all beings with God and humanity in a heartfelt way, then not only will world unity be achieved, but also the unity of heaven and earth will be realized. If human thought is like this, how much more so will be the thoughts of the one who created this heaven and earth based on the creation ideology? It must be so.

Then what kind of relationship did God establish with heaven, earth, and humanity when He created all things? Humanity must come to a conclusion about this. If there is a victorious hero who can conclude that heaven, earth, God, and humanity are one and must be united sentimentally, then his body will be the body of God, and his heart will be the heart of God. In that sense, Jesus said, "I and the Father are one."

God created all beings based on sentiment, so there is not a single thing that exists outside of God's sentiment. Therefore, Jesus came to this earth to find the focal point of sentiment with God and to prepare that place, saying, "I am the Son of God, the only begotten." Messiah! Just calling Him the Messiah? He is not just any Messiah. Many great figures or prophets have come and gone in history, but who has ever said such things? Who has ever called himself the bridegroom and referred to humanity as the bride and children? There is meaning in this.

So, where is the family that can connect with God's sentiment, apart from any social system centered on any ideology or thought? Where is the person who can connect with God's sentiment? Where are the children who can connect with God's sentiment? Where are the people and humanity who can connect with God's sentiment? Where is the person who can sing of eternal happiness through a sense of purpose and risk their life to enjoy it? There is none. Therefore, we must be saved. We are such beings.

If God has set a purpose and given life to humanity, He would not want to leave that life as it is. If we delve deeper into the content of life, sentiment emerges. Sentiment is love. It is life and love. Therefore, we advocate for life and love. What God desires until today is to establish a world of love with humans who have become true beings of life under His sense of purpose. However, such a world has not yet been realized.

To reach the world of purpose

Then what did Jesus leave behind? He left behind love. Faith, hope, and love will always be present, but the greatest of these is love. What does that mean? It means that to reach the world of purpose, God's love is necessary.

Dear friends, does anyone who has received God's love even once fall away from God? Do they oppose God? That cannot be. If a human has loved someone, they cannot forget them even in death, let alone someone who has experienced God's love that transcends the world of purpose. This is why Jesus was able to bless his enemies.

It cannot transition as it is. Therefore, there must be a great transformation. Look at the Bible. In any religious scripture on this earth, it concludes with a great transformation. A great transformation.

Eternal recognition and experience
People like to see everything with their eyes. Regardless of whether they are emperors sitting on high thrones or beggars, all humans like life-giving things. Is that not so? The level of recognition may differ according to the height or depth of perception, but the liking itself is the same for everyone. In this way, art and culture emerged to unify seeing and hearing into one.

When viewing the painting of a great artist, what should one be able to see through that painting? One should be able to see the world. Only then can one become a world-class artist. The same goes for listening. Music that becomes tiresome after one listen is not a masterpiece. A true masterpiece must be enjoyable whether one is angry, sad, suffering, or rejoicing. It must transcend time. It must transcend eras. No one can deny this.

All sensations that come through the five senses are the same for all humans. Whether they are Easterners or Westerners, civilized or uncivilized, if they are human, it is the same. There may be differences in degree, but the essence of analyzing and determining value is the same.

If God created humans to sense everything through the five senses, and if the happiness felt through those senses ends up being temporary, then that God would not be an ideal creator. He would be a temporal creator, a limited creator.

Even if it is difficult in reality, if we think abstractly, everything created by God should contain something that can be eternally experienced by anyone, whether they are uncivilized or civilized. This is the same for both hearing and feeling. Only then can God be called an ideal and absolute being. That is the truth.

From that perspective, there is something that goes beyond the consciousness and recognition that comes through the five senses, which is the intuitive conscience. Kant clearly stated this. If humans capture that world and open the door to it, experiencing something intuitive and inspirational from there, then what they have seen once will never be forgotten, even in dreams. What they have seen can last for a thousand years. This is why today’s mystics dedicate their lives to asserting their experience of the spiritual world. It is how it is.

Music, once heard, should evoke eternal emotion. Once one is immersed, it should feel like the end. The highest idealism is to make humans feel that way. It must transcend time and surpass living environments to reach a world of global emotions. This is the path that idealists must traverse.

If humans were created as beings that synthesize heaven, earth, God, and humanity, capable of feeling, experiencing, and discerning everything, then God is a magnificent creator. It is from here that the term "Dao" (道) becomes possible.

Where does God gather heaven, humanity, and earth? He gathers them into one world through a sense of purpose. With what? With the life-giving content that can govern our consciousness and ideas. Then the question is how to connect this life-giving content with inner consciousness and ideas, and what is needed here is love.

Many people on this earth have cried out for love, but no one has experienced God's love that transcends the sense of purpose. The one who came as the bridegroom to shock humanity so that they could realize that love is Jesus. Jesus, who represented heaven, was the one who possessed God. Since God, who governs heaven and earth, entered Jesus, He was a being capable of governing the world, a being that could turn the world upside down. The ideology of Jesus is the ideology of God and humanity. This must culminate in the existence of "I." Therefore, God has been coming to humanity with a life-giving standard, namely love, until today.

Humanity must find the lost world
So what position do we hold today, and what should we do? We are moving towards the world of purpose. This is because God is pushing humanity into that world of purpose. If the sons and daughters of God, equipped with the connections of life and love through a sense of purpose, appear, then the world of purpose will be realized. We must realize that world.

Then what world will come next? A world where heaven, earth, and humanity are united will come. A world will emerge where everything springs forth from God's sentiment, and connections are established and reconciled through the focal point of that sentiment. A world of sentimental connections will come. A world will emerge where the Creator is the Father and humanity are the sons and daughters, forming a familial bond.

From the day heaven and earth were created, God has longed for such a world, but due to humanity's fall, that world has not been realized. God and Jesus had to establish a love connection, and Jesus and the Holy Spirit had to establish a love connection to eliminate the world of Satan. However, even until today, such a victorious standard has not been established.

What Jesus and the Holy Spirit did was to save you. They resurrected life. This is because to achieve the purpose of resurrection, the purpose of love must also be fulfilled. From this perspective, how much has God longed for the day when He created Adam and Eve 6,000 years ago? Most people today think that God created humans as fully grown beings capable of riding horses. However, that is not the case. They were created according to the laws of nature.

Cain and Abel, born from our ancestors Adam and Eve, were not children born centered on God's love. Adam and Eve are our ancestors who were driven away by God's whip. They are our ancestors. Originally, Adam and Eve should have received the blessing from God saying, "Beloved Adam, beloved Eve, I created you to build the world of the purpose of creation of the universe, the garden of love; you are the kings of peace and happiness." No other being on this earth could become a king. Only our ancestors should have become kings. Adam could have stood as the king of the earth and the king of heaven for eternity. <Word> The title I wish to share with you is "Jesus Who Came and Goes." I will speak for a moment on the title "Jesus Who Came and Goes," not "Jesus Who Came and Went."

The reason we need a faith and a Savior
We say that God's work is a work of restoration. It is a history of finding what was lost, a history in which God seeks to find the humans lost due to the fall through His providence. If there had been no fall, there would be no need for a providence of salvation, no need for the noun "Savior," and no need for a faith that must be approached from an objective standpoint regarding the absolute God.

So why do we need faith, salvation, and even a Savior? It is because we have lost our original selves and are bound by the condition to restore them.

Throughout the long history of 4,000 years, God sent prophets to the Israelite people, who could not believe even when established or could not find direction, to announce that He would send the Messiah, the leader of the nation and the Savior of humanity. 

From the day the Israelite people left the land of Canaan, even facing the oppression in Egypt and collapsing in the wilderness, they believed that the Messiah would come. We know well through history that they hoped for a day when God would find the nation and establish a nation to govern.

The Israelite people, who were guided in this way, were in a position to follow God's command to die if told to die and to face difficulties when difficulties arose. However, even as the chosen people, they could not stand in a position aligned with God's heart due to their lineage as descendants of the fallen.

We are well aware of this fact.

What is it that God is seeking in a nation and people?
What God seeks is not merely a nation that has the outward form of a people, nor is it a nation that has only the outward form of a state. God seeks a nation that can move that people, and a state with sovereignty that can move that sovereignty, connected by heart, one sovereignty, one people, and one nation.

If they are the chosen people, they should have known who God is and for what purpose they were established. Thus, they should have pushed through any suffering and trials they faced. This was the attitude that the Israelite people should have taken at that time and the standard of heart they should have toward heaven.

However, the Israelite people, who boasted of being the chosen people, committed many sins before heaven throughout history. Of course, we must first recognize that the sin against God's heart, which was moving that era, was greater than the crimes of that era itself.

So what must God restore first in restoring humanity? Beyond desires and circumstances, we must restore the heart. We must restore the world of heart that cannot be cut off or divided. Therefore, heaven has labored behind the scenes to expand the foundation of heart at every turn of history, looking toward that one day. 

We must understand this fact today, and we must harbor a heart of indignation toward our ancestors who did not know this.

Even if we live in a tangled living environment with various circumstances, it will all eventually pass. No matter how much someone sings of their own glory while living a happy life on earth, it will all pass away. However, for those who have lived their lives holding onto a mission, there is something that remains. What is that? It is the heart that can govern circumstances. 

We cannot deny that this heart governs history, inspires national spirit, and connects thoughts.

The prerequisite for restoring humanity
Now, if what God seeks at the end is a standard of heart, then let us become the true owners of that heart. There must be true sons who can do so. If there is no day when I can say, "My beloved son," to such a son, and if no son and daughter representing heaven and earth can be established, then the coming of Jesus was in vain, and the providence of God that has been carried out for 6,000 years is in vain, and the fact that the ideal of happiness was established for humanity must also return to nothing.

Looking at the words of the text, we can see that Jesus did not come for humanity, nor did he come to walk the path of various sufferings. He came as the heavenly prince, the Savior of all people, and the protagonist of the entire creation. God sent Jesus as one who could represent God's heart, one whom God could boast about, one whom all people could revere as the representative of all hearts, and one who would be sung of by all creation as the Messiah and Savior.

Although Jesus' living environment should have been able to sing centered on heaven's heart, it was the opposite. Even in such an environment, Jesus was afraid that his own earnest heart, which had to stand before all people representing heaven and earth, would be distorted. He could not show his anger even when he was indignant. He could not show his sorrow even when he was sad, nor could he express his grievances. It was not because Jesus had too much compassion, too much mercy, or too much tolerance that he did not speak.

As the embodiment of all people who came from heaven to earth, if Jesus had acted as he wished, the conditions would have been set in the sinful world, and if he had moved as he wanted, he would have fallen into the conditions of Satan's accusations. 

He was greatly concerned that there might be any blemish in the conditions of the heart that Jesus had toward God and the heart that Jesus had toward the people he was set to lead, and the heart he had toward the universe. Jesus taught to love even enemies and had the capacity to bless enemies.

However, the history of Christianity was not centered solely on love. God also does not deal with us based solely on love, mercy, and grace. That is why the day of judgment is coming.

When is the day of judgment?
So when is the day of judgment? It is not a day when we can express our circumstances. It is a day when we must realize how much God has labored for us humans, how many twists and turns He has gone through, and how much He has endured and worked to find us, and we must weep with earnest hearts.

Today, Christians believe that the day of judgment is a day when they can sing of their own circumstances, but that is not the case. They think it is a day when they can meet the Lord and worship before heaven with joyful hearts, but that is not true. All of that will pass away. Paul said, "Now these three remain: faith, hope, and love. But the greatest of these is love" (1 Corinthians 13:13). Those who are connected to heaven and can look up to heaven with a heart that resonates with heaven, and who can hold onto Jesus with that heart, will be awaited by Jesus and by heaven. 

We must understand that the day when such people are found and established will be the day of judgment at the end of the 6,000-year providence. That is why God has left words for humanity: "I am your Father, and you are my children." Jesus also said, "I am your bridegroom, and you are my bride." Furthermore, He said, "You are my friends." He urged us to bless even our enemies while pouring out all His blood and flesh.

What are these words based on? Jesus, who was deeply moved by the heavenly heart, had the responsibility to hold onto the nation and act on behalf of that nation. That was not a joyful and happy responsibility. It was one that had to bear sorrow, resentment, and indignation. He prayed for the nation that had betrayed him with the heart that was determined to fight alone against the history of resentment. 

You must understand the heart of Jesus, who made excuses for all the rebels who drove him away. History does not just pass by.

Looking back at Jesus from 2,000 years ago, he was merely a young man. He was a trivial existence that could not catch the eye of any priest, teacher of the law, or scribe at that time. He had not learned much. He was the son of a carpenter, and even his brothers did not know he was the Messiah.

From such a standpoint, we know that he was less than John the Baptist, less than the Jews in keeping the law, and less than the scribes in action. 

How could such a Jesus become the Messiah of all people and the Savior of the universe? It was not because of his excellent appearance, nor was it because of his impressive background and power, nor was it because of the crowds that surrounded him. There was only one condition: he passed through the heart of the heavenly principle that flows through the ages. You must understand that this became the condition for all humanity throughout history to revere him as the Messiah.

We believe in Jesus, who died on the cross. We believe in Jesus, who bled and died. However, in the static world, there is no death. In the static world, one transcends history. In the world of static heart, one transcends time and space. When the heart of heaven moves, heaven and earth must move. This is the principle of creation.

Therefore, we must believe in the heart of the cross. And we must long for the saints who believe in it. We must recognize the need for a minister who can convey the heart of the cross.

Due to the fall of humanity, the issues concerning the tangled circumstances and hopes can be forgiven by God a million times, but we must understand that He will not forgive the issues of the heart.

Understanding Jesus' heart
If we, the saints, have set out to believe in the cross and connect with heaven, we must hold onto the sorrowful circumstances of Jesus and weep. We must understand the heart of Jesus, who could not weep even when he wanted to, the heart that had to pray for enemies even in a place of resentment and indignation, and the heart of Jesus, who came as the protagonist of the universe and said that everything was accomplished as he departed.

To remove the heart of God that has flowed historically through the 66 books of the Bible is unthinkable. If that happens, the value of the word will disappear.

Jesus, who came with the providence of restoration over 4,000 years, was a sorrowful person. Why? Not because he had no family, nor because he had no parents or relatives, nor because he had no nation or people. He was pitiful because he could not establish a heart connection on earth.

When we enter into such a realm and trace the circumstances of Jesus, we can understand the heart that says, "Foxes have dens and birds have nests, but the Son of Man has no place to lay his head" (Luke 9:58). We must recognize that Jesus, who hurriedly moved about, could not find a moment of comfort where he could share his heart.

Beloved, while it is good to encourage each other to believe, we must understand that a faith life that worries about God's heart is necessary.

Where must we pass through? You, who are at the end of the 6,000-year history after Jesus came and went, do you now have a friend who can hold onto heaven and speak on your behalf in the matter of the heart? And Jesus said that he is the bridegroom and you are the bride; do you indeed have a connection as a bride and groom that can make excuses even in the face of death? 

Where we must pass through.
It is important to check whether the heart of that father is in your heart and whether the emotions of that father are felt in your heart. This is crucial. You must examine this.

Two thousand years have passed since Jesus came, and six thousand years of history have flowed since Adam. We must understand that if there are no sons and daughters who can take on the heart of the Father, all the vertical connections established by God through our ancestors and Jesus in this age will become null and void. When we look at the Bible, we must recognize when Jesus felt the most resentment, injustice, and sadness, and when he faced the greatest difficulties, and we must hold onto that and become those who weep in sympathy with that heart. If there is such a person, they cannot go to hell. Even if one does not know all the words of the 66 books of the Bible, this is something that must be learned.

Jesus had a universal heart that could not be expressed. Therefore, if we are to connect with the heart of Jesus, the Savior of all mankind, we must be able to shed tears for his sad circumstances, difficult situations, and painful experiences. The thief on the right recognized the heart of Jesus as he faced death. That is why Jesus said to him, "Today you will be with me in paradise." (Luke 23:43) This was because he participated in the suffering of Jesus on an emotional level. We must realize this.

Christian believers must be able to mourn infinitely. Why? Because Jesus has not yet seen a joyful day, and God has not yet seen a joyful day. God has come through a history filled with sadness, injustice, resentment, and pain. Now we must settle this history and fulfill the providence of restoration to establish a day of joy, a day of glory.

Those who are struggling to achieve this are shedding tears wherever they go. Only those whose tears come first and who transcend their own circumstances to move their hearts toward heaven can be called believers close to heaven.

Jesus came to teach what he wanted to convey. Jesus came to this earth 2,000 years ago to fulfill the promise made to the chosen people. What did he bring? What did he want to teach the people of Israel at that time? He wanted to teach them about the historical heart of God from the day humanity fell until the time he would come. He wanted to teach them that because the historical heart is this way, it must be this way. He came to establish a hopeful nation by connecting the heart of hope with the reality of life, to build the garden that God desires instead of God.

In this way, Jesus appeared before our ancestors. He came with a heart full of longing to embrace the nation on behalf of the heavenly heart. He came to inherit such a heart as a legacy. Jesus came and lived without properly eating or dressing well.

At the closing ceremony of the 3rd National Evangelist Training Conference, he spoke: "Our will has come from under a heavenly goal. Even if we are lacking, we have a connection with all humanity and the heavenly. There is nothing greater than this. Existence, value, position, and this form have emerged from the longing of history. Who do I belong to? I am not someone who should live in the fallen historical course. I do not exist as a tool of the fallen world. I am in the fallen world, but I am not of this world; I belong to the new era. Furthermore, I belong to the Father who is working hard for this. I am the Father’s, I belong to the new era, and I belong to the new nation. I must keep this in mind.

Heaven is demanding something of me. It is to build a new world. I have been given the responsibility to resolve the events that have already been disrupted. 

So what position am I in? My individual existence is indispensable. I belong to humanity, to the world, and to the Father. Though we are a lacking nation, we must have a heart of gratitude for being called. When I think about the fact that people who have voluntarily gone for the nation and the people have not been permitted, I must have a grateful heart and a humble spirit for being called and made a son.

The teacher said that he would become one who groans for heaven, and he came. Heaven has sought such a being of goodwill.

Who do I represent? Above me are my parents, and around me is the environment I am related to. I have come on behalf of heaven and earth. You must represent the Father and the ideology of the new era. The teacher must represent your life, your ideology, and heaven.

You must become the Father’s, belong to the new era, and represent this. Additionally, you must represent this institution and the teacher on a smaller scale. Then, you must carry the burden of tears and the sacrificial offering of blood and bear God upon your shoulders. You must carry the sorrow and pain. Since I am one who has taken on the tears, blood, and substance of the Father, I must not neglect any of my actions.

In this position, for whom and for what should I live? I must live for God, for the new era, and to resolve the Father’s sorrow and pain that I carry on my shoulders.

Rather than killing our enemies, we must capture and subdue them. We must conquer their lives with our hearts, bodies, and environments. We must bring about natural submission through our hearts, not through force.

We must know everything about the enemy, even the deepest depths. We must walk the path of a scout who knows sorrow, pain, and joy. Those who understand this well can determine the day when the world of Satan will perish.

Heaven is still warning us without rest. God is hoping that you will become victors.

Though I am lacking, there are great connections behind me. The issue is not knowledge. The issue is not social experience. It is something distant, but it must be felt emotionally.

Before feeling lacking, all creatures are not lacking, and you are not lacking either. No being is lacking from an individual standpoint. You must step on the parts of lack, imperfection, or incompleteness and rise.

Just as there is no difference in parental love, there is no difference in the elements of life. A disabled child does not make their parents hate them just because they long for them. It is more precious to take a position of not feeling lacking while feeling a sense of lack.

It is important to do things with all your heart, all your will, and all your sincerity. You can do this day and night. God wants to raise such individuals at the end so that before Satan, our sons and daughters can boast, saying, "We were like this."

Until now, we have been on the defensive, but from this year, we can no longer take that position.

There has been no one to stand as a substitute for the Father, and no one to fight on behalf of the Father, which is why we have been on the defensive. Now is the time to turn that around and issue a charge.

In giving this command, the issue of heart is important. Even if heaven and earth were to disappear, the relationship with the Father cannot change; we must have the heart to finish this fight and become the glorious sons and daughters of the Father.

We must receive the Father’s things and fight against Satan with what belongs to the Father. You, the trainees, must also inherit the emotional achievements of the Father.

You must carry the Father’s creation and the achievements of the fight. You must fight on behalf of the Father. Because there has been no one to entrust this to, we have received accusations from Satan until now, but in our era, we must say that we cannot tolerate this Satan.

If you go out with this determination, you will be able to overcome any obstacle. Only then can you establish a heavenly dignity as promised.
